Re-convocation of the Special Assembly of the League of Nations (Continued)

However, the Committee of Nineteen also pointed out that the provisions of Article 15, paragraph 4 of the Covenant may only be invoked by the Assembly. Therefore, if there are any further proposals from China and Japan, they may still be submitted to the Committee of Nineteen for consideration. Therefore, while preparing the report in accordance with the provisions of Article 15, paragraph 4, the path to reconciliation has not been cut off.

At the time of drafting this report, the Japanese delegation submitted new proposals to the committee. Although the proposed amendments were fewer than those submitted in December and January, there were still doubts about the meaning of these amendments (especially regarding the amendment to paragraph 4 of the first draft), which were significant. Therefore, it was necessary to ask the Japanese delegation for clarification. According to the original text of the first draft resolution, a committee was established, whose responsibility was to negotiate a solution to the case with the parties to the dispute based on the principles of Chapter 9 of the Investigation Commission report and paying attention to the recommendations of Chapter 10 of the same report. The amendment proposed by the Japanese delegation stated that "the Committee of Nineteen should be responsible for striving to jointly obtain a method of reconciliation of the case with the parties to the dispute. The method obtained should be based on the principles and conclusions of Chapter 9 of the Investigation Commission report and apply these principles and conclusions to the events that have already developed."

The Committee of Nineteen believes that the scope of this proposal by Japan should be clearly defined. If the method of resolution is started based on a misunderstanding, it would be unsuitable for the League of Nations and its members. China has clearly explained its views on the current authorities in Manchuria. The investigation team sent to the area by the Executive Yuan has also clearly explained its nature. In the successive debates of the Assembly, the general opinion is that the solution to this case should be sought in the principles stated in Chapter 9 of the Investigation Commission report. Does the Japanese government accept the general opinion of the League of Nations, or does it still insist on its views when it first submitted the amendment, arguing that Principles 7 and 8 should not be discussed? In order to avoid misunderstandings, the Committee of Nineteen asked Japan whether the Japanese government recognized Principle 7 of Chapter 9 of the Investigation Commission report as one of the bases for reconciliation. This question was raised to the Japanese delegation on February 8.

After receiving the above question, the Japanese delegation replied on the 14th of the same month that the Japanese government firmly believes that the only guarantee of peace in the Far East is the maintenance and recognition of "Manchukuo," and that the entire Sino-Japanese dispute will eventually be resolved on this basis. In this regard, the Committee of Nineteen, although extremely regrettable, cannot but recognize that its efforts at reconciliation have been exhausted and can no longer be of service.

The above is the current situation of the League of Nations. Since September 21, 1931, the Executive Yuan in the past and the Assembly in the future have strived to pursue a solution that can be agreed upon by both parties in accordance with the provisions of the Covenant. This is exactly seventeen months. When the dispute first arose, the Executive Yuan received a guarantee from the Japanese side that the withdrawal of Japanese troops from the South Manchuria Railway area, which was already beginning at that time, would be completed as quickly as possible within the possible range.

Today, the three eastern provinces have been occupied, Japanese troops are attacking Shanhaiguan along the Great Wall, and activities to occupy Rehe are also said to be in preparation.

The method of reconciliation in this case, of course, cannot be considered to have been cut off before the Assembly passes the report in accordance with the provisions of Article 15, paragraph 4 of the Covenant. However, I am reluctant to call on both parties to make further efforts at reconciliation, because in order to achieve success, it is not only necessary to have new proposals that can be accepted by the Assembly, but also the Assembly must first obtain guarantees that the current situation will not become more severe and that military actions will not occur again.

However, I am reluctant to propose that the Assembly consider this report today. At this critical moment, we should not act hastily. The report was only distributed to the members last Friday, and governments should be given sufficient time to transmit instructions to their delegations. I suggest that the Assembly reconvene next Friday, the 24th, to begin discussing this draft report."

Careful consideration of the above text, although it does not explicitly condemn Japan, the crime of undermining mediation is undeniable. (Sent from Geneva on February 22)

Hunan National Salvation Loan

Committee established on schedule, principal and interest to be repaid in twenty years

Changsha correspondence: Hunan is raising a national salvation loan of five million yuan to serve as funds for national disaster relief and maintaining provincial defense. The annual interest rate is 4%, and the field tax of the entire province of Hunan is used as the repayment fund. Starting from the 24th year of the Republic, it will be repaid in installments over 20 years by drawing lots. The face value is divided into six types: five yuan, ten yuan, fifty yuan, one hundred yuan, five hundred yuan, and one thousand yuan. Each county and city in the province has established a national salvation loan raising committee. In Changsha City, it is organized by the Municipal Government Office, the Municipal Party Department, the Standing Committee members, the Standing Committee members of the Municipal Education Association, and five impartial gentry appointed by the Director of the Municipal Government Office as members. In addition, the 75 counties are organized by the county magistrate of each county, the director of the Provincial Tax Collection Bureau, the standing committee members of the County Party Department, the security team leader or the deputy director of the household regiment, the director of the Finance Bureau, the director of the Public Security Bureau, the director of the Education Bureau, the chairman of the County Chamber of Commerce, and three to five impartial gentry appointed by the county magistrate of each county as members. All are required to be established on April 1st and start raising funds, and the full amount must be raised by the end of June this year. It is estimated that Changsha City will be assigned to raise 300,000 yuan, and the rest of the counties will be assigned to raise at least 10,000 yuan depending on the situation, and the rest may be 50,000 or 100,000 yuan. A National Salvation Loan Supervision Committee will be established in the province, with Peng Guojun, Xie Zuyuan, Cao Dianqiu, Huang Daheng, Zhang Muguan, Peng Zhaohuang, Chen Runlin, Zhao Heng, Xie Guozhao, Liu Yuezhi, Zhou Anhan, Peng Shidi, Meng Qingxuan, Li Jingtao, and Xiao Enzhen, fifteen impartial gentry recommended by the joint conference of the Party, government and military, as members to keep the loan and supervise its use. If it is not used to relieve national disasters and maintain provincial defense, the committee may refuse to pay. The repayment and interest payment schedule for all national salvation loans has been determined and announced by the provincial government. (March 20)

Six years ago, Japan's production volume was the ninth in the world, last year it became four times that amount, and this year it is second only to the United States, accounting for the second largest in the world. Five years ago, the United Kingdom exceeded Japan by eight times, but last year Japan was three times more than the United Kingdom. The reason for this is that labor costs are low. Female workers in the United Kingdom are eight times more expensive than in Japan, and male workers are ten times more expensive. Therefore, it is greatly affected. As for tariff barriers, they are not a problem. From this point of view, the Yellow Peril warned by the former German Emperor is now coming true. The danger of Japan coercing industrial civilization with low wages is even greater than its military threat. Countries that want to maintain reasonable standards of national life should adopt a policy of not allowing goods produced by slave labor to be imported into the country.

Page 9

National Government Amnesty

Zheng Jicheng Released from Prison

(Determined to Go to the Front Lines to Kill the Enemy)

Jinan Correspondence: Zheng Jicheng assassinated Zhang Zongchang at Jinan Jinpu Railway Station on September 3rd last year, avenging his stepfather Zheng Jinsheng. After the incident, Zheng surrendered himself to the station's law enforcement team and was detained that evening at the Third Route Army's Military Law Office. On the 26th of that month, he was transferred from the Military Law Office to the Jinan Local Court Prosecutor's Office for trial. After several court interrogations, Zheng directly admitted to the assassination. On October 29th, the Prosecutor's Office filed a public prosecution against Zheng Jicheng for premeditated murder. After two court debates, the court sentenced Zheng Jicheng guilty of premeditated murder, punishable by death. However, due to his self-surrender and extenuating circumstances, he was sentenced to seven years imprisonment and seven years deprivation of civil rights. Zheng initially declared his dissatisfaction and appealed to the Shandong High Court. Subsequently, the Provincial Party Headquarters, local public organizations, and various dignitaries, due to Zhang Zongchang's various crimes during his lifetime, all praised Zheng's actions and sent telegrams to the Central Government, requesting a pardon for Zheng, so that law and human sentiment could be reconciled. Zheng Jicheng also requested to withdraw his appeal and awaited the Central Government's decision. For the sake of prudence, the Judicial Yuan specially reviewed the entire file of the case. The High Court then sent the entire case file to Beijing on February 2nd. After several studies, the Judicial Yuan finally submitted a request to the National Government for Zheng to be pardoned. On the 11th, the National Government issued a special pardon order, instructing the Judicial Yuan to order the Shandong High Court to execute it. Only today (the 20th) was Zheng brought out of the detention center and released home. Counting from September 26th last year, when Zheng entered prison, to March 20th this year, when he was released, he spent less than half a year in prison. All sectors of Jinan specially welcomed Zheng upon his release and presented him with gifts. Furthermore, when Zheng was not yet released, he expressed his willingness to destroy his home to save the country in the face of the approaching foreign invasion after regaining his freedom. Now that he has been released, he may soon fulfill his previous words and work hard to save the country. The circumstances before and after Zheng's release are recorded as follows:

(Wu Zhenzan's Conversation) The reporter heard that Zheng would be released and return home today, so he specially visited Wu Zhenzan, the president of the Shandong High Court, to inquire about everything. According to his statement, "I have been a judge for more than ten years, and Zheng Jicheng is the first case I have handled for a special pardon. Since Zheng has received a special pardon from the Central Government, all formalities can be waived. After receiving the Judicial Yuan's instructions, this court has ordered the local court prosecutor's office to handle it accordingly. There should be no delay, and he can be released and return home today."

(Judicial Yuan Instruction) National Government Judicial Yuan Instruction, Instruction No. 57, to Wu Zhenzan, President of the Shandong High Court, for compliance. The case of Zheng Jicheng's murder and sentencing to imprisonment was previously reviewed by this Yuan, and a request for a pardon was submitted. Now, the National Government's Civil Service Office's public letter of the 14th of this month states, "The National Government orders, according to the Judicial Yuan's report, Zheng Jicheng assassinated Zhang at the station because his stepfather Zheng Jinsheng was killed by Zhang Zongchang. Afterwards, he surrendered himself to the law enforcement officers. He violated criminal law for avenging his father, which is understandable. Now, party headquarters of various provinces, cities, and counties, and various mass organizations have requested a special pardon. All original sentences of the said offender are requested to be exempted from execution in accordance with the law to show compassion." It should be approved immediately, and in accordance with Article 6 of the revised Organic Law of the National Government of the Republic of China, it is hereby declared that Zheng Jicheng, who was originally sentenced to seven years of fixed-term imprisonment, is granted a special pardon to exempt him from execution to show compassion. This order, etc., is hereby recorded and sent to the aforementioned court for compliance. The case files and evidence are returned. This order, a total of eleven case files and one piece of evidence are returned.

(Local Prosecutor's Office Court Session) At 3:30 PM on the 2nd, the Local Court Prosecutor's Office held the second investigation session. The prosecutors present were Zhu Weiran and Zhu Fengxiang. Zheng was brought to the court from the detention center. Zheng was still wearing a silk gray-green cotton robe, with a gray cloth gown on the outside, and bareheaded. After arriving at the court, the prosecutors first asked his name and age, and he answered, Zheng Jicheng, forty-one years old, from Beixindian, Licheng County, residing at No. 8 Caiyuanzi Street and No. 7 Bianzhi Alley in the city. Before the murder, he was the director of the Charity Association. Prosecutor Zhu Weiran said, "Today's hearing is for your case of killing Zhang Zongchang. On October 29th last year, this office filed a lawsuit, and the local court sentenced you to seven years of imprisonment and seven years of deprivation of civil rights. The number of days of detention before the sentence was commuted at a rate of two days for one day. Afterwards, you appealed, and then you requested to withdraw it during the second instance. Now, the Judicial Yuan has submitted a request to the National Government for a special pardon, and the pardon order has arrived. Your imprisonment will not be executed, and you can leave immediately." Zheng said that the appeal was under a woman's name. Zhu said that relatives could appeal. Zheng asked if there were any official matters concerning him. Zhu replied, "No." Zheng then signed and left the court. There were many onlookers outside the court, showing the public's attention to Zheng.

(Go to the Front Lines to Kill the Enemy) After leaving the court, Zheng spoke with reporters, stating that his uncle (Zheng Jinsheng) and he were revolutionaries who should not bear grudges even when killed. However, Zhang Zongchang should not have killed his uncle and then tried to kill him, and ransacked his home six times, so he had to kill him. Zhang Zongchang was a counter-revolutionary, and his son has now surrendered to a puppet state, also becoming a counter-revolutionary. Having killed Zongchang before, he should now kill his son. Therefore, he is determined to devote his personal strength to go to the Rehe front lines to kill the enemy. Although he currently has no weapons, the anti-Japanese generals Song Zheyuan and Pang Bingxun are old comrades-in-arms, and he can go there to serve, even at the cost of his life. Because he is originally a revolutionary soldier and cannot lose his true colors. His family is destitute, his old mother is still alive, his brother Jihe and his younger brother Jizhi are both businessmen, his wife Li Shuyun, and his two sons are both deceased. His uncle's family has four young brothers, Jichun, Jiquan, and others, who have only a few dozen acres of ancestral land, and their lives are extremely difficult. But he has never cared about family matters. In recent years, while in Jinan, Chairman Han, Shi Hanzhang (You San), and Wen Boting (Mayor of Jinan) were old friends who provided continuous support. Even after entering the detention center, he relied on them for his livelihood. The warden Ren Shiwu, the chief warden Ren Xuetao, and all the staff treated him exceptionally well, for which he is deeply grateful. (20th)

Qing City

The Reality of the Stopgap Project for Tap Water

No Water Shortage This Summer, No Worries About Avoiding the Heat

Qingdao Correspondence: The Municipal Public Works Bureau's Waterworks has now published the actual situation of the stopgap project for tap water, stating, "This city has been developing year by year, and commerce and industry have been gradually prospering. Public land has been widely opened, resulting in a surge in construction and a rapid increase in the population. The sales of tap water have been increasing day by day. In recent years, wells and machines have been added to ensure that the water supply is not lacking. Due to financial and time constraints, all facilities have not been fully completed, so the increase in water volume is ultimately limited. Once there is a drought and the water source is short, or when there is a particularly large amount of water used in the summer, supply often cannot meet demand. Last summer, the hot period was longer, and the consumption of water was too large, resulting in a particularly severe water shortage. The higher areas often suffered from water outages due to excessive anti-pressure. Furthermore, the water distribution pipes on the roads were mostly installed during the German administration and have been in use for more than thirty years. The interior is mostly silted and rusted, greatly reducing the capacity and causing significant obstruction. During the water shortage period, the water flow was even more unsatisfactory. The Zhan Shan area is far from the city, and most of the water passing through the water distribution pipes is used along the way. Also, because the original water distribution pipe in that area had too small a diameter, it could not store and transport a large amount of water, so the shortage was even more acute. Although the difficult period of water shortage was勉强 overcome at that time by taking urgent measures, the plant deeply regrets the hardship suffered by the citizens due to this water shortage. To make the water supply sufficient, we must wait for开源疏浚 to be effective. In order to achieve this goal, the plant has been actively carrying out plans and rushing to complete unfinished projects, and to make supplementary facilities. The construction of various projects is listed below:

(Regarding Various Aspects of 开源) (1) Completed five newly dug brick wells in the west river of the Baisha River water source area, and installed 520 meters of water absorption pipes, so that the water at the bottom of the downstream river can converge into the west plant collection well. A 160-horsepower electric water lifting machine is added to the machine room of the well to fully attract water. It is estimated that the water volume can be increased by more than 3,000 tons per day. (2) The discharge of the emergency wells No. 4 and 5 downstream of the Licun water source is extremely strong, but due to the lack of old equipment, water cannot be sent as much as possible. Now, more than 1,000 meters of 150 mm diameter iron pipes have been modified, and a water lifting machine and a vacuum machine have been added. Also, Emergency Well No. 1 has been repaired and equipped, and auxiliary machines and water inlet pipes have been added to the machine room of the collection well. The above three wells are fully opened to increase the water level of the collection well, which can also increase the water volume by more than 2,000 tons per day. (3) A water lifting machine room is built between the two newly dug wells north of Taipingjiao, equipped with a 5-horsepower electric water lifting machine, and a water tower is set up at the high end of the south to prepare for pumping well water to the water tower to supplement the lack of water in the Zhan Shan area. It is estimated that the water volume can also be increased by several hundred tons per day.

(Regarding Various Aspects of 浚流) (1) The Baisha River water source is about 20 kilometers away from the Storage Mountain, and the reservoir on the Storage Mountain is about 70 meters above sea level. The water from the water source is delivered through a long distance of 20 kilometers, and then climbs a high mountain of 70 meters, resisting the static water pressure of the reservoir. Therefore, although the pressure of the water lifting machine at the water source reaches the maximum limit, it is still difficult to increase the water volume. Now, a reservoir of several thousand cubic meters is added next to Mongolia Road, and a machine room is built, equipped with three 160-horsepower electric water lifting machines, so that the water sent from the water source flows smoothly into the pool, and then it is pumped to the Storage Mountain Pool, so that the pressure is reduced and water delivery is convenient. The city can get an additional 3,000 to 4,000 tons of water per day. (2) There is an existing reservoir next to Taiping Mountain Road that can store 200 tons of water. It is now being repaired and a 125 mm water pipe is installed to connect with the Wendeng Road and Taipingjiao water supply pipes. A water stop gate is installed there, so that when the pressure is high at night, water can enter the pool for storage, and when the pressure is low during the day, water can flow out of the pool to supplement the lack of water in the Taipingjiao area. (3) A 125 mm diameter water pipe from the old one in front of the Municipal Middle School is connected to the water distribution pipes in Taipingjiao and Zhan Shan roads, so that the water sent from the city can be branched out smoothly. With the addition of the Taiping Mountain Road Reservoir and the Taipingjiao Water Tower, the Zhan Shan area can avoid the risk of water shortage. (4) Replace the 125 mm water distribution pipe from the Taishan Road intersection, via Dengzhou Road, to the north end of Yindao Road with a 200 mm water pipe, and connect it with the Licun water supply trunk pipe. During the summer season, the water gate at the junction can be opened to allow the water from the Licun water source to be directly injected into Qidong Road, Laiwu Road, etc. without going through the Storage Mountain, and the water gates in the Jinshuo Road area with higher area, which are connected to the water distribution pipes in the lower areas of the city, can be closed at the same time to prevent the water from flowing downwards, thus facilitating water use in high places. (5) Increase the water distribution pipes on Yindao Road and Qihe Road to connect with the Fushan Road pipeline, so that the water use in higher areas on Fushan Road and Qixia Road can be supplied through the new water pipe on Dengzhou Road, the same as Qidong Road and Laiwu Road. (6) A 125 mm water pipe is added between Guanhai Road and Guanxiang Mountain, one end connected to the downward water pipe of the Guanxiang Mountain Reservoir, and the other end connected to the Guanhaishan water distribution pipe. When there is a water shortage in summer, the water gate between Guanhai Road and Pingyuan Road can be closed, and the water gate of the Guanxiang Mountain Reservoir can be opened to allow the water stored in the pool to be supplied to Guanxiangshan Road and Guanhai 1st and 2nd Roads through the newly installed water pipe. (7)通洩 and replace the heavily silted water distribution pipes on Taiping University, Laiyang, Anhui and other roads, so that water can be fully distributed to avoid the problem of insufficient water flow on various roads in the city.

The above various projects cost a total of more than 200,000 yuan. In addition, the fundamental solution for a large-capacity reservoir's water source has also been started. Regardless of when the project can be effective, even in terms of the existing stopgap project, it is expected that the summer water shortage can be avoided in the future.

International Chamber of Commerce Conference

Our Country Decides to Stop Participating

A Telegram Will Be Sent to Paris Soon

The Seventh International Chamber of Commerce Conference is scheduled to be held in Vienna on May 29th. The Chinese branch recently decided to stop attending this conference because of the national crisis and the participants are unwilling to go. A telegram will be sent to the Paris headquarters soon to state the reasons for the absence.

Aviation Association Establishes Aviation School

School Site Has Been Negotiated

Borrowing Hongqiao Airport

The Chinese Aviation Association will establish an aviation school to develop China's aviation industry and cultivate civil aviation talents. This proposal has been planned for a long time. The directors of the association believe that Shanghai is the most suitable place for the school site because Shanghai is the most developed commercial port in China. It is convenient to hire professors and purchase equipment, and the Aviation Association's headquarters is in Shanghai, so the management of the school will not be alienated. However, Shanghai lacks a large enough place for training. After discussion at the Standing Committee, it was decided to borrow the Hongqiao Airport of the Aviation Administration and temporarily borrow the training aircraft of the administration for teaching. Therefore, Lin Wojiang, the secretary-general of the association, was specially sent to Hangzhou to contact Ge Jingen, the director of the Aviation Administration. Lin returned to Shanghai the night before last. The reporter specially interviewed him about the negotiation process. According to him, Director Ge has agreed to borrow the site, but the borrowing of training aircraft is still under negotiation. Therefore, a meeting of the Standing Committee will be convened soon to report the negotiation process, and then discuss the next steps. Director Ge is very concerned about the association, so he also offered advice to establish a aircraft factory, starting from a small scale, whether it is self-made or repaired, to achieve the goal of self-made and self-repair. This idea is very good, so it will be reported to the Standing Committee for discussion.

Telegrams of Bitter Battles Outside the Pass

Condolences to Anti-Japanese Generals

The Northeast Volunteers Support Association received telegrams from Commander Sun Dianying and Chairman Song Mingxuan yesterday, as well as various incoming and outgoing telegrams. The combined records are as follows:

I am deeply grateful to the gentlemen for their enthusiastic donations. The entire army will be even more motivated to supervise the troops and fight to the death with the Japanese pirates. The enemy has been reinforcing our Liangdigou positions in recent days and attacking our positions with cavalry, tanks, and field battles from time to time. In order to save ammunition, our soldiers calmly respond to the battle when the enemy comes to attack, and often do not return the guns. When the enemy rushes to the front, they rush out of the trenches and kill the enemy with big knives and hand grenades. White-blade hand-to-hand combat is most terrifying to the enemy. It is estimated that three enemy tanks have been destroyed and many trophies have been seized. This is specially telegraphed to express my gratitude. Sun Kuiyuan叩, 馬,

The Disarmament Conference Actually Restricts Our Air Force Development

China's Number of Aircraft Only One-Fifth of Japan's, Leaving Us Without Self-Defense Capability; Resolutely Oppose

The World Disarmament Conference has reached a deadlock due to the issue of restricting air forces. Recently, British Prime Minister MacDonald and Foreign Minister Simon proposed standards for restricting air forces, stipulating that the five major powers (Britain, the United States, France, Italy, and Japan) should not exceed 500 aircraft, with other countries decreasing proportionally. China is limited to no more than 100 aircraft. The Disarmament Conference is scheduled to convene today (yesterday's telegram mentioned a postponement). Whether the proposal will pass and whether it can be implemented after passage remain uncertain. However, the people's call for national salvation through aviation deserves deep attention. Lin Wo-jiang, Secretary-General of the Aviation Association, told a New Sound News Agency reporter yesterday morning that China's coastline is extremely long and its borders vast, while its army and navy equipment cannot compare with those of the great powers. If the air force is further restricted, it will effectively place China in a position where it cannot defend itself. The people should resolutely oppose this. China's current air force is less than 100 aircraft. Whether we can build an air force sufficient for self-defense depends on the efforts of the people and the government. However, there is a huge difference between this and being restricted by international forces and unable to establish one at all.

Zhu Turns Liu Telegram: All colleagues are informed. I have just received a telegram from Commander Liu of Shimentown as follows: General Zhu Ziqiao, Greetings. After the enemy facing Shancha Ridge was repelled by us last night, I immediately sent a team to track and attack, clearing the battlefield and capturing more than a hundred steel helmets, countless backpacks and military supplies. We also found Manchurian maps, orders, diaries, and other items on the body of Colonel Shimamura, who died in battle. It has been confirmed that eight officers above the rank of captain were wounded or killed in this battle, including Captain Yoshida and Colonel Hayakawa. The enemy has now retreated to the vicinity of Banbi Mountain and is building fortifications. I am sending this telegram to you. Your humble servant, Liu Ruming, bows in respect, etc. Transmitted by Zhu Qinglan, Ma Wei-zong.

Yangzhen Telegram (titles omitted): I left the pass last year to investigate the true situation of the anti-Japanese civilians. Details have already been sent to Shanghai for publication. The Japanese army occupied our Chaoyang and Lingyuan counties because Tang's army retreated without a fight, preventing the national salvation army from providing support. Now, the armed civilians of the entire Rehe province are rising up to unite, consolidating strategic passes, and awaiting the opportunity to kill the enemy. We are currently in a period of shortage, during the season of continuous spring rain, lacking urgently needed supplies such as military raincoats, undershirts, uniforms, flour, salted fish, marching pots, and stoves. We hope that you will all join in overcoming national difficulties, assign personnel to solicit contributions, accumulate provisions, and transport them to the front lines to support the patriotic soldiers, encouraging their courage to kill the enemy and achieve results. This telegram is urgent. Wishing you daily peace. From Yang Zhen of Rehe, respectfully.

Telegram of Condolences to Song and Guan: The Shanghai Citizens' Federation sent a telegram yesterday to Army Commander Song and Division Commander Guan, stating: Greetings to Chairman Song Zheyuan and Division Commander Guan Linzheng of the Beiping Military Branch. Conversations with a Returnee from Shenyang

The Tragic State of the People in the Northeast

A reporter from the Datong News Agency recently met with Mr. Wang Maosheng, who had secretly escaped from Shenyang to Shanghai, at his lodging. He recounted the tragic situation of the Japanese army's treatment of the people in the Northeast, filled with tears and blood, which was unbearable to hear. The details are recorded as follows:

The Current State of the Puppet Regime: Mr. Wang began by saying that recently, after the Japanese army suffered heavy losses in attacking Xifengkou, the Japanese troops stationed in various parts of the puppet regime have been ordered to go to Rehe, reaching more than three divisions. This has left the internal defenses of the puppet regime extremely empty. Only a small number of Japanese military police and Chinese troops who have betrayed the country are maintaining local order in various places. Since the news of the Japanese army's defeat reached Manchuria, officials of all ranks in the puppet organization have been panicked. In addition, the guerrillas, who have broken up into smaller units, are lurking in various places, firing their guns at night as a show of force, further unsettling the puppet officials. In order to calm themselves, the puppet army immediately requested and received permission from the highest Japanese military authorities to transfer more than 4,000 military police from Korea and send them to various places to monitor the people, preventing them from secretly colluding with the guerrillas and launching surprise attacks. At the same time, the Japanese military authorities, fearing that the traitorous army might take restless actions, secretly deployed Japanese troops near the traitorous Chinese army, ostensibly to assist in maintaining security, but in reality to monitor them. As for the Japanese residents, due to the dangerous situation, they also spontaneously organized self-defense groups, which were formally established at the beginning of this month. The group has about 500 members, and weapons were obtained from the puppet military and political department. On the 14th of this month, the overseas Chinese military and political department, after receiving repeated telegrams of the Japanese army's defeat in Rehe, immediately declared special martial law. Residents were not allowed to go out after 5:00 p.m. During the day, pedestrians on the street were not allowed to talk to each other in groups of three or more, otherwise they would be punished with extreme penalties for disrupting public order and inciting popular discontent. Their state of panic has reached an extreme point.

Strict Prohibition of Free Entry and Exit: Mr. Wang also said that the Manchurian puppet organization has recently been very strict in preventing residents from freely entering and leaving the territory. The purpose is to prevent plainclothes guerrilla units from infiltrating the interior. Anyone wishing to leave the territory must first provide detailed reasons and submit two full-body photos and a joint guarantee from two local shops to the local government.

The Future of the Guerrillas is Worrisome: Since the outbreak of the Rehe War, the Manchurian Japanese military authorities have adopted a policy of massacre against the guerrillas in various places, and have implemented a blockade to cut off the guerrillas' supplies. Although the guerrillas scattered throughout Manchuria have broken up into smaller units and are lurking in deep mountains and valleys, their food supplies have long been cut off and they are only living on wild vegetables. The Japanese army is sparing no effort in searching and killing them. Every time they capture a guerrilla, they are subjected to dismemberment by five horses or hung upside down from the treetops to let their blood flow downwards and die. If they encounter women, the young ones are first raped and then hacked to death with random knives, while the elderly are subjected to cruel instruments of torture and die. The tragic state is something I (Mr. Wang refers to himself) really cannot bear to describe again. If our government authorities do not recover Rehe as soon as possible and open up the supply route for the guerrillas, then hundreds of thousands of Chinese heroes will be lost to the hands of the Japanese pirates. I sincerely hope that the government officials will make a painful decision, issue a national mobilization order as soon as possible, and quickly leave the pass to recover the lost territory in order to save the people of the four provinces who are being trampled under the iron heel of the Japanese army and the hundreds of thousands of guerrillas who are sacrificing themselves for the country.

Ma Xiangbo, the Old Man of Ninety-Four

Initiates the Society of Those Who Cannot Bear to See Suffering

Hopes Fellow Citizens Will Emulate Father Lebbe and Participate in Implementation

Yesterday's newspaper reported that Father Lebbe, who has been living in China for thirty years, responded to Ma Xiangbo's founding of the Society of Those Who Cannot Bear to See Suffering by personally leading the first batch of rescue teams to the front lines of Xifengkou. A reporter from the New Sound News Agency made a special visit to Mr. Ma Xiangbo, the old man of ninety-four, and had the following conversation: (Reporter asked) Did the old gentleman initiate the "Society of Those Who Cannot Bear to See Suffering?" (Answer) Indeed, I initiated this action on November 11th of last year, specifically to rescue all the suffering compatriots in the war zones of the Northeast and the bandit areas of the South. I entrusted the Tianjin Yishibao to take charge of the event, and a large amount of cash and cotton clothing were raised, all of which were given to the National Salvation Association of Tianjin. Unfortunately, I am old and frail, able to speak but unable to act. My old friend Father Lebbe, in view of the bloodshed and death of the soldiers on the front lines, is actually showing the compassionate heart of "those who cannot bear to see suffering" and forming a rescue team. Father Lebbe is a highly respected clergyman internationally, so his personal trip to the front lines to carry out work is better than the empty talk on paper of the Peace Army advocated by London. I am also just talking on paper, but I hope that my fellow citizens will emulate Father Lebbe's implementation. (Question) What are the old gentleman's thoughts on the current situation? (Answer) Yesterday, I read in the newspaper that Mr. Wang Jingwei, in his first speech after returning to China, said that he was thinking of the hard work and sacrifices of the anti-Japanese soldiers on the front lines, and immediately expressed his deepest respect. At the same time, President Yu of the Supervisory Yuan also gave a lecture at the National Government, also to comfort the patriotic soldiers on the front lines, which shows that national opinion is unified and the whole nation is resisting foreign aggression and saving the country. We know that the soldiers on the front lines are respectable and lovable, but those who sacrifice themselves for resisting Japan are naturally even more lamentable and worthy of song. In order to reduce the suffering of the loyal and brave soldiers who sacrifice themselves for national salvation, in order to show that all compatriots unanimously do not forget the merits of the soldiers on the front lines, and to go to the front lines to carry out rescue work, such as the righteous actions promoted by Father Lebbe, will leave a deep impression in the minds of those who are saving the country, like the heroes of the anti-Japanese war at Xifengkou. According to the old man's observation, this kind of rescue team is no different from a suicide squad, because the Japanese army's atrocities have always disregarded the civilized customs of Europe and the United States, and often openly violated international laws of war, such as the bombing of ambulance vehicles and the killing of rescue teams during the previous Shanghai battles, which were recorded in detail in the Shanghai newspapers. However, in Shanghai, there were still various countries watching, and they were slightly more cautious. Now, in the illegal warfare outside the pass, they are doing everything possible. Therefore, I hope that all fellow citizens in the country will not forget the brave soldiers who are resisting the enemy, unite to help and provide frequent rescue. From the ruling personnel to the civilians, for the sake of the life and death of the country, they should all act like suicide squads and go to the front lines. Father Lebbe's trip is just a vanguard, not only promoting the spirit of Catholic universal love, but also in line with the ancient morality of "not inflicting heavy wounds" in the righteous wars of the Spring and Autumn period. I urge all fellow citizens to participate in the implementation together.

Continued Arrival

Antiquities Shipped Out Last Night

According to the Central News Agency, 1,290 boxes of the second batch of antiquities from the Palace Museum being shipped south, along with 1,064 boxes of the first batch stored in Beijing, and 200 boxes of antiquities from the Ministry of Interior's Antiquities Exhibition Hall, totaling 2,554 boxes, arrived in Shanghai on the Kuaili, a vessel of the China Merchants Steam Navigation Company, after being loaded from Beijing around 2:00 p.m. the day before yesterday. Due to the short time on that day, they could not be unloaded, so it was decided to start unloading yesterday morning. However, it rained heavily yesterday morning, and it did not clear until nearly noon, so the unloading was delayed until about 12:00 p.m. More than a dozen trucks from the Mao Tai and Shanghai搬场 Automobile Companies, and dozens of laborers, were divided into loading and unloading points. When the unloading began, the French Concession Police sent several Vietnamese police officers to the four corners of the Jinliyuan Pier to control pedestrians and vehicles entering and leaving the crossroads. Personnel were stationed along the route to ensure solemnity. The unloading was completed at 6:00 p.m. Currently, there are 3,608 boxes of antiquities stored in the warehouse at No. 26 Tianzhutang Street, with no remaining space to store the third batch of antiquities. As for the company of soldiers escorting the artifacts, their company commander, Zhao Zhong, is scheduled to return to Beijing on the original ship this morning.

Northeast Thaws and Opens for Navigation, Huge Amounts of Food Shipped Out

Two Million Bags of Flour

Forty to Fifty Thousand Bags of White Rice

Yingkou and Andong in the Northeast have been closed due to freezing since last winter, with navigation suspended for more than three months. Yesterday, the ice began to thaw, and Shanghai's merchant ships also resumed navigation to Yingkou yesterday. However, at the beginning of this thawing and opening of ships, Shanghai suddenly had a large amount of rice, flour, and other grains transported to the puppet regime. This matter is not only related to the people's livelihood but also violates the ban. Our reporter made a special trip to investigate the matter, and the details are as follows:

(Ordering Large Quantities of Flour and Rice) At this time when the Japanese army is mobilizing to attack Rehe, the front lines need a huge amount of food. It is said that the Japanese army in the north eats rice, while the puppet Manchurian army eats flour. Therefore, the Northeast has recently come to Shanghai to purchase a large amount of flour, more than two million bags, mostly under the Yuanbing Chuan brand. They also secretly purchased 40,000 to 50,000 bags of white rice. The destinations are divided into two places. Before Yingkou thawed, it was loaded to Dalian. Now that Yingkou has thawed, it is directly loaded from Shanghai to that port for unloading. Various Shanghai Chinese and British merchants' ships are competing to load, including Haichang, Yu Da, Taifeng, Datong, Zhaoxing, Zhengji, and Taigu and other shipping companies.

(Navigation Resumes Yesterday) A telegram from Yingkou stated that the port has thawed and is scheduled to open on the 25th of this month. Shanghai ships began loading cargo to Yingkou yesterday. Datong Company's Tongsheng ship transported 2,400 bags of white rice and 104,000 bags of flour yesterday. Taigu's Zhejiang ship also carried more than 100,000 bags of flour. Taifeng's Fengxiang also sailed to Yingkou yesterday. According to the Jianghai Customs, it has long been forbidden to transport food to the Northeast, and the Ministry of Communications has also instructed various shipping bureaus not to load food to Anyinglian and other ports in the puppet regime. It is unknown how the customs is handling this.

(Forced Registration of Crew Members) When Yingkou and Andong were closed due to the river freezing last winter, the puppet regime issued a puppet order stating that when Chinese merchant ships arrive at the sea ports of the puppet regime, in addition to paying taxes, etc., Chinese ships sailing to Yingkou and Andong must also have the puppet customs inspect the ship and issue an inspection certificate before they can sail. It also ordered all Chinese ships arriving at Yingkou to register their crew members with the puppet regime, paying a registration fee of two to five yuan per person. The method is the same as our country's regulations. This time, it must be forcibly implemented.

(Situation of Strict Inspection) Dalian has banned the import of Chinese newspapers from Shanghai. If anyone is found carrying them, they will be heavily fined. Chinese people going to Dalian, Yingkou, or Andong from Shanghai must undergo special searches. In addition to unloading and inspecting luggage, even the lining of clothes and the lining of hats must be cut open on the spot with a knife and inspected by Japanese detectives, and viewed against the sunlight. If there is any discrepancy, they will be considered spies and arrested, and their lives will be difficult to protect.

American Church

Also Affected by the Financial Storm

Missionaries Will Generally Have Salaries Reduced

According to the North-China Daily News, after the financial storm in the United States, the American churches propagating in China may also reduce their activities. It is reported that many churches have received telegrams from the United States, notifying them of the need for further salary reductions. Yesterday, a gentleman from the American Methodist Church told a reporter that, to his knowledge, various churches in the United States may generally reduce salaries by at least 25%. According to the salaries of the churches, they have previously been reduced, and the number of missionaries has also been reduced successively since 1927. It is feared that the number of people remaining in China is only half of what it was in 1927. Furthermore, those missionaries who request long vacations often cancel them in order to save money. Most of those who will return to China soon are those who will not return to China after their leave expires. However, the overall situation is still uncertain, and it is hoped that by June, it may return to normal.

The Ministry of Finance Approves Exemption from Affixing Stamps for Shipping Notes in the Transportation Industry

The Ministry of Finance Approves Exemption from Affixing Stamps

The Municipal Chamber of Commerce submitted a request from the Transportation Industry Association to the Ministry of Finance to allow exemption from affixing stamps on shipping notes. The Chamber immediately forwarded the request for exemption. It has now been learned that the Ministry of Finance has approved the request. The Ministry's response states: We have received your report. The shipping notes issued by the transportation industry are temporary notes issued by the shipping company to the carriers to ask the stores transporting goods to send the goods. They are not a substitute for the bill of lading or formal receipt. Since the bills of lading, etc., are all stamped in accordance with regulations, the shipping notes should be exempted from stamping. In addition to instructing the Jiangsu Stamp Tax and Tobacco and Alcohol Tax Bureau to comply with this, you are instructed to forward this order for notification. This approval.

Meeting of the National Products Promotion Committee

The Shanghai First District Citizens' Federation held its third National Products Promotion Committee meeting at 2 p.m. yesterday. Twenty-one people attended, including Zhen Binghui, Liu Zhongying, Zhou Fuzhang, Zhang Yichen, Hu Fengxiang, and Chen Jicheng. (5) Regarding the organization of a National Products Promotion Lecture Team, it was resolved that the Publicity Section should plan and implement it. The meeting adjourned at 5 p.m.

Ministry of Industry and Fisheries Association

Levy of Fishery Construction Fees

Collection Rules Have Been Approved and Promulgated

Provisional Rules for the Collection of Fishery Construction Fees by the Fishery Improvement Committee of the Ministry of Industry for the Jiangsu and Zhejiang Regions: (1) These rules are formulated in accordance with the provisions of Article 3, Paragraph 2 of the Committee's Organization Regulations. (2) The rate of levy for fishery construction fees shall be 2% of the market value of the fishery products, limited to one time. (3) All fishery products, whether fresh, salted, dried, or shellfish, shall pay fishery construction fees in accordance with these regulations. (4) The collection of fishery construction fees for fishery products shall start at 100 catties. Those who are less than this amount or who are scattered shoulder-pole vendors shall be exempt from the levy. (5) The collection of fishery construction fees shall be entrusted to the fish markets for collection. When necessary, the Fishery Improvement Committee of the Jiangsu and Zhejiang Regions may set up offices for collection. The expenses shall not exceed 5% of the fees collected. The fees collected in the preceding paragraph shall be submitted to the Fishery Improvement Committee of the Jiangsu and Zhejiang Regions for safekeeping before the fifth day of the following month. (6) A four-part form shall be filled out for the collection of fishery construction fees. One part shall be given to the fish merchant, one part shall be kept at the collection office, and two parts shall be submitted separately to the Ministry of Industry and the Fishery Improvement Committee of the Jiangsu and Zhejiang Regions. The forms in the preceding paragraph shall be pre-printed by the Ministry of Industry and stamped with the official seal of the Fishery Improvement Committee of the Jiangsu and Zhejiang Regions. (7) Those who fail to report the levy or report the levy incorrectly may be punished by the collecting agency or auditor, depending on the circumstances. The penalty rules shall be formulated separately. (8) The detailed rules for the implementation of these rules shall be drafted by the Committee and submitted to the Ministry of Industry for approval. (9) These rules shall come into effect on the date of approval by the Ministry of Industry.

Qu Wenliu to Regularly Go North for Disaster Relief

Yesterday's Broadcast Appealed to All Circles for Donations

Qu Wenliu, a standing director of the Shanghai Charity Organizations United Association for Relief of Northeastern Refugees, believes that the disaster in the Northeast urgently needs relief. He is scheduled to go north on the 25th of this month. Yesterday, he made a special broadcast on the Asia-America Radio to request generous donations from all circles. His words are recorded below.

"Reflecting on Mr. Ying Guang's previous broadcast at the Shanghai Broadcasting Radio Station, he reported on his personal visit to the Qinhuangdao area for disaster relief and the dispersal of people in the war zones. If we do not rush to provide relief, the soldiers will arrive and the people will leave, which is no different from strengthening the walls and clearing the fields ourselves, putting our compatriots on the front lines in mortal danger. I think you can still remember that the failure at Rehe and Gubeikou was due to the soldiers not being able to protect the people, and the people not being able to share the same hatred with the enemy. Now, refugees from Lingyuan, Kailu, Fuxin, Jianping, Chaoyang, Suidong, Beipiao, Nanling and other places within Rehe are fleeing inward in groups. The people of Zunhua and Jixian within Xifengkou, and Miyun and Huairou within Gubeikou, are constantly bombarded by airplanes and burned and killed, as the front lines are in fierce battle. If we do not urgently settle them, there will be bloody battles in the front, and escapes in the rear. People will have no support in life, no treatment for injuries, and no place to rest in death. It is not only a loss of land, but also a loss of our race. It is painful to speak of, and brings tears to think of. Alas, it is terrible!

Our association has repeatedly received reports from Feng Yangshan, a disaster relief specialist at the front lines, stating that refugees in the war zones are gathering together, lacking clothing and food, and having no place to live. To flee would be to disregard the soldiers on the front lines, which is unacceptable. To stay would be to share the soldiers' clothing and food, which would inevitably lead to mutual destruction. He requested that a large amount of relief supplies be urgently raised for prompt assistance. Therefore, we have appointed Mr. Ying Guang to continue to go north for disaster relief, to fulfill the obligations of a citizen. Mr. Ying Guang has previously traveled to the front lines and our office knows the situation well. I feel that I cannot refuse this duty, so I have decided to go north immediately. However, the scale of this disaster is unprecedented and cannot be alleviated with a small amount of relief funds and supplies. I respectfully ask all the elders, brothers, sisters, and aunts and uncles of the country to have compassion for the hungry and drowning, and generously donate. Donate one more yuan, and you can save one more life. Save one day earlier, and you can preserve one more point of vitality. I, Ying Guang, vow to purely use the nature of charity and humanitarianism to perform this arduous task for all the great philanthropists, to save our disaster victims. I sincerely bid farewell and beg you nine times over!"

Unemployed Marine Engineers

Petitioned the Maritime Affairs Bureau Yesterday

The Shanghai Chinese Marine Engineer and Driver Association recently learned that the Ministry of Communications stipulated that only those with nautical knowledge and experience are allowed to serve as marine engineers on ships, and that the ministry will issue qualified employment certificates. However, in order to save costs, shipping companies have replaced certified engineers with people who have no knowledge at all, resulting in as many as 100 unemployed engineers. Yesterday, unemployed marine engineers sent more than 20 representatives, including Li Ronghua, Mao Jinquan, Zhou Yeyuan, Wang Shiyong, and Xu Wencai, to the Maritime Affairs Bureau of the Ministry of Communications to petition for the elimination of unqualified marine engineers to maintain the livelihood of workers. Yu Boming, the section chief of the second section of the bureau, received them and promised to start handling the matter within one month, eliminating unqualified marine engineers. He also stated that if the company continues to use unqualified engineers who have not been inspected, the bureau will refuse to inspect them. According to the workers, if the elimination is not carried out after one month, they will petition the Ministry of Communications again.

Therefore, we hereby inform you to investigate and pray that you will inform all members that in the future, if there are insurance matters, please contact the office as much as possible.

Original Verdict Upheld in Indian Police Murder Case

Two Indian Police Officers in Hankou File Another Appeal

In the case of Indian police officer You Sha, who blocked Hong Kaifa, a tenant of the third room, from moving out and stabbed Zhou Ayu to death in Li Zhongli, the defendant refused to accept the ten-year prison sentence imposed by the first-level court and appealed to the British Assize Court. The appeals court ruled the day before yesterday to uphold the original verdict. However, considering that You Sha was young, it was conditionally permitted that if he behaved well in prison and repented, he could petition the British Minister to China for a reduction in his sentence.

At the same time, two Indian gatekeepers in Hankou, due to religious disputes, gathered eight people to fight in the streets of Hankou. The court sentenced them to one year in prison and ordered them to be deported after their release. They also appealed against the deportation order, requesting reconsideration, claiming that the defendants had sold all their property in India and brought their families to China. Now, in China, they may still have outstanding loans that have not been recovered. The deportation for a minor fight may lead to their bankruptcy. This case was also heard in the British Assize Court the day before yesterday.

Shanghai

Ningbo Industrial Bank Shareholders' Meeting

The Shanghai Ningbo Industrial Bank has been operating quite well since its establishment in October two years ago. On the 19th of this month, a regular shareholders' meeting was held in the bank. A total of 148 shareholders attended, which was sufficient for a quorum. The meeting was called to order and Wu Zhihao was elected chairman. He reported on the business situation of the bank and its branches, stating that when the bank was established two years ago, it coincided with the January 28 Incident in Shanghai. For the sake of prudence with the shareholders' capital, the directors of the bank only chose to make secure loans. As a result, the bank did not suffer any losses. When the situation stabilized, the bank officially opened on June 4 last year. However, it still adhered to the principle of stability, so it has achieved considerable results since its opening, which is gratifying. The bank's settlement account for last year has been audited and certified by Xu Yongzuo, a famous Shanghai accountant, and has been sent to the supervisors for review and stamping. A separate account statement has now been prepared and submitted to the shareholders for their perusal. Subsequently, Supervisor Lin Kanghou reported, stating that the business situation of the bank has been reported in detail by the chairman, which should be understood. The bank's accounts have been audited by accountant Xu Yongzuo and have been reviewed and stamped by this supervisor. There are no errors, so please rest assured. After the reports were completed, the settlement for the 21st year was approved on the spot, and three supervisors were re-elected. The results of the ballot were that Lin Kanghou, He Shaoyu, and Guo Yonglan were re-elected. The meeting adjourned when the bell rang six times.

Public Works Department

February Health Report

The February report of the Health Officer of the Public Works Department stated:

The mortality rate for foreigners this month was 14.21, compared to 13.07 last month. The increase was due to more deaths from tuberculosis and pneumonia. The mortality rate for Chinese was 16.99, compared to 14.79 last month. The increase was mainly due to the discovery of more deaths on the road.

The birth statistics showed that 32 birth reports were received for foreigners this month, and 153 for Chinese, of which only 114 were living within the boundary. This statistic cannot be improved until hospitals and midwives are fully registered.

This month, 10,009 people were vaccinated against smallpox, of which 7,323 were handled by the injection car and 2,686 by the district health centers.

The number of influenza cases has increased recently. Generally speaking, although the severity of this disease varies from person to person, the danger is that it may cause pneumonia, which can be life-threatening. Moreover, those who suffer from this flu often feel unwell for weeks or months. Therefore, those who suffer from it should not treat it as the same as a common cold.

The pathological research laboratory conducted 1,577 tests this month. The rabies treatment room had 39 consultations, of which two came from other cities.

The average daily milk production was 26,170 pounds. The number of inspections was higher than usual, as a new factory opened and another factory resumed operations after reorganization. Buffalo milk and local cow's milk were also inspected and analyzed several times, and the results were satisfactory. Twenty-seven sick cows were found and removed, and compensation of approximately 378 yuan was paid.

Business at the small vegetable markets was slightly worse after the Lunar New Year, but it has recovered in the middle of this month. The weights and measures used by the vendors were checked and compared as usual. Only one case of violation was found and prosecuted.

The cleaning department of the Health Department was as busy as usual with vaccinations and investigations of infectious diseases. Inspections of schools and factories were carried out as usual. The cleaning of outdoor swimming pools has also begun.

Miyun County, Hebei Province

Temporary Women and Children Relief Society Established

According to news from the Shanghai Chinese Children's Welfare Association, the Temporary Women and Children Relief Society has been formally established in Miyun County, Hebei Province. Zhang Jinghe, a priest of the local Catholic Church, was elected as the president by the local residents, and Wang Youan, the assistant manager of Tianxing Gold Mine, was elected as the vice president to handle the reception of women and children. The letter from the Relief Society requesting assistance from all parties is listed below:

"Dear Sir/Madam,

Due to the outbreak of the war in Rehe, the people have lost their homes and jobs, have no place to live, and have no way to go. It is difficult to count the number of people who have died from freezing and starvation. The large army along the way has passed through the area frequently, and the people have fled. Nine out of ten houses are empty. When our colleagues witnessed this chaotic situation, they were angry and heartbroken. Therefore, we initiated the organization of the Women and Children Relief Society, which has been open for more than ten days. We have already taken in more than 400 women and children. If this continues, the number of people will inevitably increase. At present, we are running out of resources, but we cannot bear to stop. It is difficult to sustain this situation. We have long heard that your organization is compassionate and can help those in distress. If you can generously provide assistance to save the victims, our association and the women and children we have taken in will be grateful for your great kindness."

The End of the Butterfly and Snow Affair

| Lin Xuehuai Has Repaid His Debts |

The Butterfly and Snow Affair, which caused a sensation for a time, has been going on for three years. The part of Hu Die's request to dissolve the marriage contract with Lin Xuehuai has been finalized after three trials. As for the part requiring Lin Xuehuai to return the debt, the original amount was more than 4,000 yuan, but the court ruled that he should repay more than 600 yuan. Lin has not fulfilled this obligation for a long time. Recently, Hu Die's attorney, Zhan Jifeng, filed a petition with the First Special District Local Court for prompt enforcement. On the day of the hearing, Lin Xuehuai was operating a photography business in Suzhou and did not know about the case, so he did not appear in court. The execution judge then approved the plaintiff's request and waited for the document to send the police to Suzhou with the plaintiff to identify and arrest him. After the newspaper reported this, Lin finally learned of the matter and quickly returned to Shanghai to settle the debt. The arrest will not happen, and the marriage drama will come to an end from now on.

Pitiful Unemployed Man Kills Himself

A man with improper clothing came to the Tangshan New Hotel at 342 Tangshan Road at 12 o'clock late the day before yesterday and booked a room. He wrote his name Chen Ziying, from Ningbo, 28 years old, in the circulation book. Later, he secretly took opium and committed suicide. At about 8 a.m. the next morning, Zhang Hequan, the tea servant, was cleaning the room next door and heard the man moaning constantly, so he knew something was wrong. He immediately went to inspect and saw that he could not speak, was foaming at the mouth, and saw an opium box and other items on the table. The tea servant immediately reported to the accountant, who reported to the Huishan police station and ordered Chinese detective Bao Desen to investigate. He was sent to Tongren Hospital for treatment, but he died shortly afterwards. A suicide note was found by his side, which stated: "I am a poor man who is unemployed and homeless. I hope the authorities will report the body for collection." The detective then took the body to the Feilun Road morgue. Yesterday morning, he reported to the First Special District Local Court and appointed Prosecutor Guo Wei to inspect the body. After taking the seat, Mr. Guo ruled that the deceased Chen Ziying had died of opium poisoning. The body was handed over to the Pushan Villa for collection.
