German Automobile Mechanic and Wife

Travel Around the World, Passing Through Shanghai

Driving a British Austin Seven Car

On October 20th of last year, German automobile mechanic Mr. Blanc and his wife, Ms. Dono, set off on a grand journey around the world in a new British-made Austin Seven car. They traveled smoothly through Austria, Hungary, Yugoslavia, Bulgaria, and reached Arabia. They then traversed the 600-mile desert region between Damascus and Baghdad, with sandstorms obscuring their vision, and the car windows had to remain closed. Upon reaching Persia, the roads deteriorated further, but fortunately, they did not encounter any bandits along the way. They arrived in Quetta, the capital of Balochistan, which is one of the hottest places in the world. The city is modern, but few Europeans visit. After arriving in Calcutta, they rested for ten days, then took a boat to Rangoon, reaching Penang. They continued by car to Singapore, then by boat to Saigon. They disembarked and traveled to Haiphong, intending to travel overland through China and Nanning in Guangxi, but were hindered by heavy rain. They returned to Annam and took a boat to Hong Kong. They then boarded the President Cleveland and arrived in Shanghai the day before yesterday (the 20th). Accompanied by Mr. Cruz, General Manager of the Shanghai Ford Motor Company, Mr. Bowen, General Manager of the American Tong Motor Company, and Mr. Lin Zhenbin, General Manager of the Huashang Advertising Company, they toured Shanghai for a week. Yesterday, they took the same ship to Japan. They will also travel to the United States and then return to their country via England. Mr. and Mrs. Blanc highly praised the performance of the Austin Seven car, stating that they had traveled over 12,000 miles without any need for repairs.

The Thirteen-Year-Old

Missing Girl Incident

丨Abducted and Sold to Fujian by Maternal Uncle in Collusion with Three Women丨

Gui Bao, the thirteen-year-old daughter of Mrs. Wang Le, a Ningbo native residing at No. 46 Zhaofeng Road, is a beautiful and charming girl. She was studying at the Muyi School of the Methodist Church on Huilu, attending evening classes for two hours. On December 21st of last year, at around 8 pm, she went to school but did not return. Mrs. Wang went to the school to investigate and was told that a man in his thirties, with a large face and nose, wearing a blue cloth short-sleeved shirt and trousers, had taken her away. Mrs. Wang did not recognize this person and searched everywhere, but to no avail. According to intelligence reports, the police searched for the abductor without success. Mrs. Wang wept day and night, but could not find any clues. Recently, Mrs. Zhang Le, a relative from Ningbo, came to Shanghai and learned that the girl Le Guibao had been abducted by her maternal uncle, Le Wenxing, in collusion with Ningbo women Gong Li (also known as A'er), Chai Lu (also known as A'yu), and Li Liu (also known as A'mao Niang), residing at No. 147 Aierkaoke Road, Dongyouheng Road, No. 38 Yuqing Lane, and No. 8 Lishou Lane, and sold to a wealthy man named Zhang in Nancang, Xinghua County, Fujian Province. They received 300 yuan, which they divided and spent. Mrs. Wang secretly reported this to the Huishan Concession Police the day before yesterday. Detective Li Hongsheng was dispatched and arrested the three women at their addresses, taking them back to the police station and transferring them to the women's prison for temporary detention. Yesterday morning, they were escorted to the Third Criminal Court of the First Special District Court. Police lawyer Zhang Tianyin described the events in detail and requested a postponement. After Mrs. Wang Le provided her testimony, Judge Wu Zehan questioned the defendants briefly and ordered them to remain in custody, with a rescheduled hearing date to be determined.

A Peiping Woman

Demands 60,000 Yuan in Damages

Filing a Criminal Complaint, Shandong Native Song Lizhai is Required to Compensate for Emotional and Material Losses

Li Xiangru, a 23-year-old woman from Peiping, is of sound physique and fashionable attire and is skilled in Peking opera. In the winter of the previous year, she met Song Lizhai, a native of Shandong, at a social gathering. They began living together at No. 30 Yonganfang, Yongan Street, in the French Concession, and later moved to No. 68 Siming Lane, Xiahfei Road. Song, however, was already married. His attitude towards Li was solely based on money. Recently, Li ran out of money and was unable to provide for Song's extravagant spending, so he abandoned her. Li, believing that Song had committed an act violating Article 244 of the Criminal Code, hired a lawyer to file a criminal complaint with the First Special District Court, along with a civil suit, demanding 60,000 yuan in compensation for emotional and material losses. Yesterday afternoon, Judge Xiao Xiefei opened the Third Criminal Court for the hearing. The defendant was absent. His lawyer appeared in court and stated that the defendant had gone to the capital on business and would be able to arrive in Shanghai in three or four days. He requested that the court grant a postponement. Judge Xiao granted the defendant's lawyer's request, rescheduling the hearing for the 25th and informing them that if the defendant failed to appear at the next hearing, the court would issue a warrant for his arrest.

The Press Association

Replies to Letter from Members Gu Zhian and Others

Explaining Misunderstandings in the Letter, Statement Also Made by Chairman of the General Assembly

The Shanghai News Reporters Association replied yesterday to a letter from members Gu Zhian and thirty others. In addition,

A letter from Gu Zhian and twelve others to the Association was also issued, with a statement included below.

Reply from the Press Association: Gentlemen, we received your letter expressing doubts about the recent election and requesting to withdraw from the Association. After reading it repeatedly, we are deeply saddened. The Association was originally formed through the reorganization of the Shanghai News Reporters Federation. At that time, due to the dismissal of staff by the Shishi Xinbao without justifiable reason, we sought to obtain a legal basis for the organization itself, in order to consolidate its internal unity and improve the soundness of its organization. Hence, the decision to reorganize was made. After legitimate preparation, it was legitimately established. Fortunately, the total number of members reached 199. This is the largest number of members for a reporters' organization in the city since its establishment. If all members work together, we might be able to achieve even a tenth of our organizational goals. Unfortunately, misunderstandings arose at the recent meeting, which all members deeply regret. Thirty members of the Association, out of a total of 199, have requested to withdraw. In the Association's records, this is undoubtedly a significant loss. We sincerely hope that these thirty members, after understanding the facts, will be able to dispel their misunderstandings and restore their original membership numbers, and work together to advance the Association's affairs. This is why the Association is calmly and rationally willing to explain the matter to the thirty members. The letter from the thirty members to the Association is divided into four parts, but their only argument is that a list was discovered at the meeting, which they believe indicates electoral fraud. The letter from Mr. Huang Tianpeng and eight other members states that "this method seems close to monopolization." The letter from Mr. Gu Zhian and twelve other members states that "beforehand, there were rumors that one or two unscrupulous individuals were controlling the election." Saying "seems close to monopolization" and "rumors of manipulation," using terms of suspicion and hearsay, in correspondence and newspapers, those unfamiliar with the situation may believe that the Association's election had some kind of scandal and that the elected committee members were of low character. The members lightly used harsh words in their letters, fearing they were not exhaustive enough, leaving no room for the group of 199 members to work together, leaving no room for the character and reputation of all reporters in Shanghai, causing those who care about the Association to grieve, those who hate the Association to rejoice, and those who the Association has previously criticized to snicker. The consequences are not what the members initially anticipated. Furthermore, in terms of facts, how can the discovery of a list at the election meeting immediately be deemed as fraud? At the time, representatives from the Municipal Party Committee and the Municipal Social Affairs Bureau were present to provide guidance and clearly indicated that the list did not hinder the election process. The presidium also put to a vote whether or not to announce the list, and the majority of members indicated that they did not want it announced. Since the list was not announced, how could the members present know the names on the list? Even if the electors wanted to avoid the names on the list, how could they do so? The members who are now requesting to withdraw were mostly those who participated in the election. If they believed that the discovery of the list constituted fraud, how could they have continued to vote and elect as usual? And perhaps some of the members' ballots also included votes for people on the list. Can these members also admit to colluding in fraud or being manipulated? Since the members made no statements at the time, and only spoke of election fraud after the names of the elected officials were announced, the Association can understand that the members' actions, although lacking in restraint, may not have had malicious intent. However, outsiders will surely believe that the members themselves were not elected and are therefore making these slanderous statements and destructive actions. Can the members endure this? The members also stated that one or two unscrupulous individuals were controlling the election. Even if there were one or two unscrupulous individuals, their guilt only extends to those one or two individuals. To implicate the entire committee, let alone the Reporters Association, let alone the character of reporters, as if all but the thirty members of the 199 members were people who did not know how to cherish themselves and willingly accepted humiliation, is it not that the members think too highly of themselves and too lowly of others? Furthermore, even if, as the members pointed out, there were indeed abuses in the election and it was manipulated by one or two individuals, then the members could use their membership rights to denounce and punish the crimes of those one or two individuals. But instead, they resorted to the passive measure of withdrawing from the Association. After withdrawing, they lose their qualifications and can no longer advocate for Association affairs, tolerating the Association's affairs and the reputation of reporters being sold out and destroyed by one or two unscrupulous individuals. Are the members more concerned with the one or two unscrupulous individuals than with the entire membership? In short, a list, one or two unscrupulous individuals, based on the members' thinking, seem to believe that the Reporters Association should be sacrificed. Then how can they face the other 169 members? And how can they face the Party and government representatives who were legally present to provide guidance? The members should think about this carefully. An organization is a public entity, and only the public will should be followed. The committee members, having been legitimately elected, have legal and moral responsibilities to the members. In addition to notifying the elected committee members to assume office on time, the Association specifically explains the misunderstandings and presents a full reply. Facts are the ultimate rhetoric, and prejudice disappears after careful examination. Then the members will surely have a thorough understanding one day, and the Association also hopes to have the opportunity to work for the members again, as it did when it worked hard to resolve the dismissal crisis at the Shishi Xinbao. We have said all that we need to say. We hope you will reconsider it. We wish you all the best. The Shanghai News Reporters Association.

Statement of the Presidium: We read in the Shishi News on the 21st that Mr. Gu Zhian and twelve other members of the Association

sent a letter to the Association, in which it stated that the presidium even stated that some members of the presidium had participated in refusing to accept [the list] beforehand. Upon investigation, at the general meeting held at the Youth Association in Baxianqiao on the 18th of this month, a vote was taken on the incident of someone finding a list, and it was decided not to announce it. As for Chairman Yan Esheng saying that if the original finder believed it necessary to pursue the matter, then the list would be the only evidence and should be kept by themselves and handled according to the law, the presidium was not in a position to accept it. Would there not be a risk of the list being destroyed if someone on the presidium had participated in the matter? There was no affirmative tone of someone on the presidium participating beforehand. This is a matter of common sight and hearing. How can the meaning of the words be deliberately altered, deviating from the truth? In addition to directly writing to the members, we are afraid of confusing the hearing, so we hereby declare this for public review. Respectfully submitted by Yan Duhe, Zhao Junhao, Hang Shijun, Yan Esheng, Qu Shao Yi.

Wang Yiting and Others on

Contributions to the Berlin Chinese Art Exhibition

Hoping to Enlist Famous Artists from Across the Country so that Everyone Can Apply

Wang Yiting and others sent a letter to the "Call for Submissions to the Berlin Chinese Art Exhibition," stating: Gentlemen, we recently received your letter calling for submissions to the Berlin Chinese Art Exhibition. We are grateful for your consideration, even though we are just mediocre talents and are not worthy of the honor. We have heard that the method of soliciting submissions for this exhibition is that the committee members of your association, with a spirit of great impartiality, widely solicit works from famous artists. This is like a coral iron net, without regretting any talent being missed. However, based on our observations, we dare not be secretive and offer some humble suggestions, hoping you will adopt them. We have heard that for this call for submissions, your association has internally set a limit of only about 100 people. However, within the country, there is no lack of diligent artists with exquisite works, both in major cities and secluded areas. It is definitely not limited to the 100 people we have seen and heard of. Taking the Chinese Painting Association, which we founded, as an example, the members number more than 190. Among them, there are many with refined painting skills and superb artistry, which we cannot hope to match. However, they are not on the list of solicited artists. We are merely service personnel of this association, yet our names are mentioned and recognized, not because we have specialized skills in practical learning. If we were to simply decline, we would not be able to face the members of our association. If we were to avoid submitting, we would not be able to face your association's intention to widely solicit submissions. We are truly in a dilemma. Moreover, this is not just about our association. From a small perspective to a large one, taking the Chinese Painting Association as an example, more than a dozen members have already been solicited. Multiplying this by ten, it is not a small number. However, among the members of our association, more than 180 have talents superior to ours but harbor regret at not being selected. Based on this, how many talents are missed across the country? Missing the talents of the Chinese Painting Association is a small matter, but missing the talents of the world is a big matter. In our humble opinion, this is absolutely unacceptable. Therefore, to avoid this drawback, the only way is to completely cancel the predetermined list and create new regulations, openly soliciting submissions and strictly reviewing and selecting, so that everyone in the world can apply and have no regrets at not being selected. Your association takes talent with great impartiality and does not accept mediocre pieces. After all, the Berlin Chinese Art Exhibition is an international platform, not a private exhibition. How can the eyes and ears of a dozen committee members and the works of a hundred people be said to represent the art of the entire country? If you adopt our humble suggestions and do not hesitate to ask questions, we are extremely willing to exhaust our knowledge and offer our contributions. If you consider our arguments to be wrong, then we would rather remain reclusive and hidden, and not be guilty of failing the art of the entire country. We humbly submit our sincere feelings for your public consideration. Respectfully addressed to the Preparatory Committee of the Berlin Chinese Art Exhibition. Wang Yiting, Chen Xiaodie, He Tianjian, Wu Zhongxiong, Wang Aishi, Xie Gongzhan, Sun Xueni, Zhang Shengzhuang, Zhang Yuguang, Zheng Wuchang, Qian Shoutie, together send their regards.

National Art Exhibition

Actively Preparing for the Lottery

Remaining Donations Exceed 4,000 Yuan

The Relief Association Allocates Aid to the Righteous Army

The National Art Exhibition, jointly organized by the Northeast Volunteer Army Relief Association, the Republic of China National Salvation Organizations United Association, and the Chinese Painting Society, was previously held at the Lake Society and the Ningbo Native Place Association for a total of nine days. It has now concluded. The total revenue from both modern and antique works, as well as ticket sales, special issue catalogs, and donations from entertainment activities, amounted to 8,743.237 yuan. The expenses for preparatory meetings and costs amounted to 4,525 yuan, leaving a net income of 4,217.60 yuan. According to Mr. Hu Zusun, the executive director of the association, this income was originally entrusted by the Northeast Volunteer Army Relief Association to designated personnel to deposit in banks and allocate to the righteous army. The association itself did not receive the funds. Currently, the association is in the process of transferring the matter to the Supervisory Committee of the Relief Association for review, so that a special booklet can be published for public information and to enhance credibility. Meanwhile, the remaining works are being sorted, renumbered, and active preparations are underway for a lottery ticket sale. Mr. Hu also stated that the remaining works still number over 2,000 pieces, with many valuable works, valued at over 20,000 yuan. If 3,000 tickets can be sold at a minimum of five yuan each, it will generate 15,000 yuan. Recently, donations of works are still abundant. For example, Wang Yuwen donated two framed landscape paintings, and Wang Ming, a nine-year-old prodigy from Shanghai, also donated a couplet.

The Nanyang Tobacco Factory Dispute Continues

The Company Responds to the Conditions Yesterday

The Workers Petition the Party and Government

Following the strike at the Nanyang Brothers Tobacco Company in Hongkou, Wu Shiyuan, the arrested union officer, and worker Li A Jin were transferred to court yesterday. The company has formally responded to the conditions raised. The workers have sent representatives to petition the party and government agencies. The details are as follows:

Workers Sent to Court: After the dispute occurred, a worker named Zhang Desheng was arrested on the spot by the Hongkou Patrol Room and sent to court for trial the day before yesterday. At that time, union officer Wu Shiyuan was in the gallery next to the court and was subsequently arrested by detectives. In addition, a worker named Li A Jin was arrested in the factory. Yesterday morning, the Hongkou Patrol Room transferred them to the First Special District Court, where Judge Wu Zehan interrogated them. Nanyang Company sent legal counsel Wu Linkun to court to state the case, while the patrol room's lawyer, Zhang Tianyin, stated in court that the case was originally handled by Judge Xiao, and therefore requested a postponement to the 28th for a joint trial. The judge approved the request and ordered the two defendants to be remanded in custody.

Yu, fourteen years old, a girl Lin Mei, eighteen years old, and Zhong Yu's thirteen-year-old fiancee Xing Xian, have lived together at home since childhood (that is, a child bride and a cousin of Zhong Yu). After graduating from elementary school, Zhong Yu was introduced to a mounting and painting shop called Jiu Yi Tang at the Wangjia Pier in Nanshi last spring as an apprentice. Last autumn, he suddenly fell ill with lung disease and returned home. Medication was ineffective, and he died in the middle of the night on the fourteenth day of the first lunar month this year, 42 days ago. The next day, his family prepared a coffin and embalmed the body, and temporarily parked it on the bank in front of the Pan family's house in Hebei Town. Unexpectedly, at about 8 o'clock the night before last, Xing Xian was lying on the bed, repeatedly calling "Bitter mother, bitter mother, the child has been resurrected!" Upon hearing this, the Qiu family felt that the voice sounded like Zhong Yu's, so she rushed to the floating coffin, removed the straw, and wanted to see the face of the dead person. However, some good people took rumour-mongering as their ability. The coffin shook, there were voices inside the coffin, and the coffin lid still had residual temperature, etc., and the ghost stories were so vivid. The foolish people did not realize it and regarded it as a fact. They also said that the yang energy was heavy during the day, and they planned to open the coffin at 8 o'clock in the evening. As a result, it spread from one to ten, and from ten to a hundred. In an instant, two to three thousand people gathered. Those who like to gamble and play Huahui in Shanghai took cars to worship, running on the Shanghai-Min Road, endlessly. The head of the Third Precinct of the Sixth District of the Municipal Public Security Bureau, Liu Lun, learned of the previous situation, and was deeply afraid of undermining public order. So he sent Inspector Yuan Desheng, together with the head of the security team of the district, Ding Qingzhong, to lead the team police to suppress it. He carefully observed the girl Qiu Xingxian, her eyes were motionless, her eyebrows were upside down, and the strangest thing was that she could make a sound from her throat without moving her mouth, but it was not clear, as if she was suffering from nervous symptoms. He immediately ordered Pei Su to send Xing Xian to Shanghai for treatment. On one side, the floating coffin of the deceased was ordered to be moved to the border of Songjiang County, Henan Province for temporary placement. The sensational resurrection of the dead person was finally calmed down.

Continued Hearing of the Club Case

Jiang Boxian, who lives in Xingjuli, Nanhui Pavilion Road, and makes a living selling fancy clothes, once lost his job, so he formed a rotating credit society to raise capital. Among his members were Zhou Ronggui, who runs the Zhou Wansheng noodle shop, and his widowed sister-in-law, each with one share. Unexpectedly, in June or July of last year, Zhou's sister-in-law won a share and remarried. Jiang Boxian was unable to bear the responsibility, so he negotiated with Zhou Ronggui. Zhou agreed that there was still a small share, and they would calculate again. If the small share was won, he would find another guarantor. By the end of last year, Zhou needed money urgently, so he won the share. Jiang urged him to fulfill his promise, but Zhou refused. In the evening, he gathered people to go to Jiang's house with weapons and coerced Jiang's wife, Jiang Wu, saw him turn around at the door, and ran outside to report to policeman Liu Lindong, saying that there was a robbery at home. The policeman, without asking the reason, saw Zhou running out of the house and shot him, killing him with a shot to the head. The First Precinct of the First District took Liu Lindong, Jiang Boxian, Jiang Wu, etc., into custody and sent them to the local court. After the prosecutor investigated, he charged Liu Lindong with murder under Article 282 of the Criminal Law, and Jiang Boxian and Jiang Wu, etc., with false accusations. Yesterday morning, Judge Qian opened the court for trial. According to Liu Lindong, he shot Zhou Ronggui because Jiang Wu reported that there was a thief, I entered the door and Zhou Ronggui ran outside, in the darkness, his hand was raised, as if with a weapon, I told him to stop, so I shot upwards in self-defense, causing him to be hit in the head. Jiang Boxian was standing in the reception room, etc. Jiang Boxian said that after the deceased won the share, he asked him for a guarantor, but he had no guarantor three times. When I was having dinner, he brought two hooligans, pulled out their sleeves, and tried to rob me of my money. I quickly grabbed Zhou, but Zhou broke free and escaped. The police officer had already shot over. I did not report the police, nor did I go out. Please investigate. Jiang Wu said that she was washing clothes in the patio when those people came in to rob her, and their appearance was terrifying, so she went out to call the police. I don't know how the police officer shot Zhou Ronggui to death, etc. At this point, Chen, the lawyer hired by Jiang Boxian, said that Jiang Boxian did not report the police, nor did he go out, so he was not responsible for false accusations. He cannot be implicated because of the marital relationship. Now Jiang has a serious case of hemoptysis due to an old lung disease and requests to be released on bail for medical treatment. After the presiding judge reviewed the case, he ordered bail to be granted for further questioning and then ordered the case to be retried.

Murder Case Near the North Station

Newspaper Vendor Killed with an Ax

The deceased was specializing in the newspaper vending business on the two railway lines and the cause of the murder seemed to be related to a grudge.

At 6:15 AM yesterday, an unprecedented murder occurred at the entrance of Lane 9, Shanqing Lane, south of the North Railway Station. The deceased was Zhou Yiting, also known as Zhou Laowu, who specialized in selling newspapers from major local newspapers on the Beijing-Shanghai and Shanghai-Hangzhou-Ningbo railway lines. The identity of the murderer is currently unknown, as it was early morning, there were few pedestrians on the road, and the residents in the lane had not yet woken up. Therefore, although Zhou was killed, it is difficult to know who the murderer was and how many there were. According to the investigation, Zhou lived at No. P.190, Lane 5 in the same neighborhood, and had been in the newspaper business for two decades. He had been jointly selling major newspapers along the Beijing-Shanghai Railway line with Cheng Yinsheng, Xia Chengliang, and others. Only two months ago, he resumed selling newspapers along the Shanghai-Hangzhou-Ningbo Railway line. Zhou usually got up at 4:00 AM every day and went to the North Station to handle newspaper distribution matters. Recently, because his nephew, Zhou Quan, was able to take over his work, he sometimes went out as late as 6:00 AM. At 6:00 AM yesterday morning, Zhou went from his residence to the North Railway Station and was suddenly attacked by several thugs. Zhou was unable to defend himself and was violently hacked five times with an ax, causing him to fall to the ground. The thugs, seeing that their goal had been achieved, discarded the ax and fled. Zhou was seriously injured but still conscious. A certain old woman from the same neighborhood went out to get water and shouted for help, saying, "Old good woman, come and save me!" The old woman was shocked and saw Zhou lying in a pool of blood, with blood gushing from his forehead, covering the ground. She was greatly frightened and shouted, causing all the neighbors to wake up. They immediately tried to help him back to his home and reported the incident to the nearby police post. Subsequently, the Haining Road Patrol Room notified the Central Fire Brigade to dispatch an ambulance, accompanied by a Chinese policeman No. 1782 and Zhou's wife, Li, to the Tongren Hospital for treatment. However, due to the severity of his injuries, he died at around 9:00 AM. A reporter from the China East News Agency visited the scene yesterday after the incident. According to nearby residents, the incident appeared to be a revenge killing. When the tragedy occurred, they heard shouts for help, but they thought it was a thief being caught and attacked, so they did not want to get up. It was not until they heard the old woman's shouts that they realized something was wrong and went out to investigate, only to find that Zhou had been killed. At that time, Zhou was still able to speak. He had five ax wounds, two on the left temple and three on the back of the head, all several inches deep, resulting in significant blood loss. The murderer's ax was taken away by the police for investigation. At 11:00 AM, Chinese and Western detectives from the patrol room returned to Zhou's residence to investigate everything in the hope of obtaining clues. Zhou was 51 years old and a native of Nanjing. His wife, Li, was 40 years old and a native of Ningbo. They had a son and a daughter, the older one, Gui Tang, 7 years old, and the younger one, Gui Fen, 6 years old. Both children were lively and innocent, and as charming as ever, unaware that their father had been hacked to death. Zhou's nephew, Zhou Quan, was at the North Station when the incident occurred and rushed back to his residence upon hearing the news. He said that it was difficult to predict whether the incident was a revenge killing. Zhou had celebrated his 50th birthday on December 6th of last year and held a banquet at his residence. Not long after, he died tragically. The Haining Road Patrol Room is making every effort to investigate this case.

Storm in the City: Commotion at Changqiao

Rumors Confuse the Public: Resurrection of the Dead, Police Bureau Interferes, Temporary Relocation

There is a Pei family in Changqiao Town, West Shanghai, whose son died more than a month ago. Now, there is a sudden rumor of resurrection, and ghost stories are rampant, causing a sensation. The details are recorded below: Changqiao Town, East of the Wujia Lane Station on the Shanghai-Minnan-Zhejiang long-distance bus line, the brother of He Nanqiao, the current painting artist, the third brother Jiancheng, died nine years ago, leaving behind his sister-in-law, Qiu, who is now forty-three years old, and has three sons and one daughter, the eldest is Gen Yu, twenty years old, the second is Zhong Yu (the deceased), fifteen years old, and the youngest is Bu Qiang. As for Yu, who is fourteen years old, the girl Lin Mei, who is eighteen years old, and Zhong Yu's thirteen-year-old fiancee Xing Xian, have lived together at home since childhood (that is, a child bride and a cousin of Zhong Yu). After graduating from elementary school, Zhong Yu was introduced to a mounting and painting shop called Jiu Yi Tang at the Wangjia Pier in Nanshi last spring as an apprentice. Last autumn, he suddenly fell ill with lung disease and returned home. Medication was ineffective, and he died in the middle of the night on the fourteenth day of the first lunar month this year, 42 days ago. The next day, his family prepared a coffin and embalmed the body, and temporarily parked it on the bank in front of the Pan family's house in Hebei Town. Unexpectedly, at about 8 o'clock the night before last, Xing Xian was lying on the bed, repeatedly calling "Bitter mother, bitter mother, the child has been resurrected!" Upon hearing this, the Qiu family felt that the voice sounded like Zhong Yu's, so she rushed to the floating coffin, removed the straw, and wanted to see the face of the dead person. However, some good people took rumour-mongering as their ability. The coffin shook, there were voices inside the coffin, and the coffin lid still had residual temperature, etc., and the ghost stories were so vivid. The foolish people did not realize it and regarded it as a fact. They also said that the yang energy was heavy during the day, and they planned to open the coffin at 8 o'clock in the evening. As a result, it spread from one to ten, and from ten to a hundred. In an instant, two to three thousand people gathered. Those who like to gamble and play Huahui in Shanghai took cars to worship, running on the Shanghai-Min Road, endlessly. The head of the Third Precinct of the Sixth District of the Municipal Public Security Bureau, Liu Lun, learned of the previous situation, and was deeply afraid of undermining public order. So he sent Inspector Yuan Desheng, together with the head of the security team of the district, Ding Qingzhong, to lead the team police to suppress it. He carefully observed the girl Qiu Xingxian, her eyes were motionless, her eyebrows were upside down, and the strangest thing was that she could make a sound from her throat without moving her mouth, but it was not clear, as if she was suffering from nervous symptoms. He immediately ordered Pei Su to send Xing Xian to Shanghai for treatment. On one side, the floating coffin of the deceased was ordered to be moved to the border of Songjiang County, Henan Province for temporary placement. The sensational resurrection of the dead person was finally calmed down.

Qian Daochang, a Confucian doctor from Jiangyin, located at No. 1 Dingkang Lane, Triangle Field, Jisfeier Road, Caojiadu, has secretly manufactured more than ten kinds of miraculous medicines over the years, among which are particularly famous: Xiaor Dingjing Pills, Pain Relief Powder, Cholera Pills, Asthma Essence, Headache Powder, Qiufeng Pills, and Stop Diarrhea Water, etc. Since helping people, countless people have been saved. A while ago, wealthy businessmen Han and Ruan, etc., either suffered from asthma or phlegm, and they sought many famous doctors, but it was difficult to see results. After purchasing and taking Qian's miraculous medicine, in less than half a month, they completely eliminated the ten-year-old old ailment. Now, in order to popularize society, Qian has reduced the price of medicines, only charging costs, and the fixed price of each Dingjing pill is eighty cents, each bottle of Qiufeng pill is two yuan, each small bottle of Asthma Essence can be taken for ten days and costs five yuan, each box of Cholera pills is three yuan, each dose of Headache Powder is eight cents, and each bottle of Stop Diarrhea Water is two yuan. Reader Advisory

The Future of Normal School Graduates

丨Letter from Mr. Zhao Jiyu of this city丨

Speaking of the future prospects of normal school graduates, it is true that in the current Chinese society, they are generally looked down upon. However, we must also ask: Have the normal school graduates themselves fulfilled their due responsibilities? If they abandon their own responsibilities to seek a way out, there is no doubt that going east will be "This road is blocked," and going west will also be "This road is blocked." What are the responsibilities of normal school graduates? Let's look at how many out-of-school children there are in China today. Let's also see how many illiterate people there are. We know that these people and children have not found a way out; then, have the normal school graduates fulfilled their responsibilities? Asking ourselves honestly, if normal school graduates abandon their own responsibilities to seek other ways out, they will inevitably only find pain and frustration. It is true that everyone needs to eat, which is naturally a crucial issue. However, normal school graduates are laborers. They cannot enjoy a superior material life, and in reality, they do not enjoy it. Furthermore, they cannot rely on society to support them; they must be social producers and find a way out for society. Therefore, the responsibility of normal school graduates is to popularize production education for society. However, in today's Chinese society, this path is full of thorns. Therefore, normal school graduates must have the determination to create, the courage to pioneer, and the perseverance and hard work to overcome all obstacles. If normal school graduates take on the mission of "finding a way out for society," then they themselves will have a way out. I am also a normal school graduate, and I have been struggling in society for nearly ten years. I once wandered down another path. Regarding my recent life, it can be considered a good position, a primary school teacher earning thirty or forty yuan a month, which is quite good. However, I feel pain because I have abandoned the responsibilities of a normal school graduate, and I am just working as a hired laborer. Is this my way out? Is this the way out for us normal school graduates? As the saying goes, "We certainly cannot fight to fulfill the mission of the times on an empty stomach, but if you don't engage in this struggle, you will still go hungry." I am not going hungry now, but I want to do something, to work to find a way out for society, to be a producer for society. Therefore, I have decided to resign from my current teaching position in the second half of the year, 丨this is a school "making money for private individuals"丨 and I want to establish a school for popularizing production education. This is also to take on a bit more of the responsibility of a normal school graduate! What do you think of my idea? Can this path be taken? Mr. Yin Rixin, or other comrades, if you can jointly take on this responsibility of normal school graduates, I will naturally express my welcome twelvefold. I hope readers will sympathize with me, guide me, and help me.

Answer: Your ambition to resign from a school "making money for private individuals" and establish a school for popularizing production education is commendable. However, what exactly is a "school for popularizing production education"? To be honest, under the current political situation, it is "harder than ascending to heaven" for someone with nothing to establish a school for production education. Even if you勉strongly succeed, it will just be another school signboard on some road or lane in Shanghai, and another place to "make money" by deceiving people. This is not entirely due to the goodness or badness of people, but rather the social and political environment does not allow you to do otherwise. In my opinion, since you are going to be a laborer anyway, instead of being a word-chewing laborer in a school, you might as well go to a factory or company to be a physical or semi-physical laborer. In that environment, you may find opportunities to fulfill your obligations as a normal school graduate. As for your letter, you say "Normal school graduates are laborers" at the beginning, but then you say "I am just a hired laborer. Is this my way out? Is this the way out for us normal school graduates?" The words seem a bit contradictory. In fact, normal school graduates have no way out. If they really want a way out, the only way is for normal school graduates to consciously become laborers and fulfill their responsibilities as normal school graduates among the laborers.

Shen Bao National Products Weekly

Eleventh Issue Published Every Thursday

Introduction to New Industries

Mr. Kong Yongzhi's Impressions from Special Envoy Investigation

— Yu Qiacheng

Mr. Kong Yongzhi was previously commissioned by the government to investigate industries in Europe and America. He spent half a year and recently returned to Shanghai. The Shanghai Industrial and Commercial Management Association specially held a meeting to welcome him. During the meeting, Mr. Kong was asked to report on his impressions of the investigation. The following record is his lecture at the time. It has not been submitted to him for revision, so the reporter is still responsible for the text.

This time, being commissioned to investigate abroad happened to be during the autumn of the global economic panic, so it can be said to be fortunate and unfortunate. It is difficult to see the benefits of visiting when others cannot develop themselves. However, exploring the precedents of others and understanding the reasons for their failures cannot be said to be completely unproductive. This is like medical students who must go through difficult and complicated cases to increase their experience.

According to my personal findings, the reasons for the economic downturn in Europe can be divided into the following items:

(1) Mass Production: The United States vigorously pursued large-scale production, resulting in overproduction. Many products have become equal to waste. Now, the closed factories are unattended, and the social and economic impact of worker unemployment is significant. This is the biggest reason.

(2) Inability to Purchase: Because of the unemployment wave, the society's inability to purchase is certainly the biggest reason. However, the irrational consumption in the past is also the cause of the economic downturn. Previously, American workers could use installment payments, paying ten dollars to buy a car and five dollars to buy a piano. Such irrational consumption is also something we should be wary of.

(3) Speculative Business: Speculative business is very popular in the United States. A company can issue stocks at will, without certain restrictions. Later, stocks worth 500 dollars were only worth five dollars and no one wanted them. The government is responsible for this.

We have seen the situation of others. In the future, we can learn from the following five aspects:

(1) To prevent biological overproduction, in addition to paying attention to large-scale production, we should also pay attention to handicrafts. The government must also have precise statistics to prevent overproduction and control various industries.

(2) Demand that production and consumption are suitable and develop production industries separately according to consumer surveys.

(3) Prevent excessive speculative business. It is impossible to stop all speculative business during commercial competition, but it should be limited and cracked down on.

(4) Strive for labor-capital coordination. Germany has disputes due to labor-capital problems, which have affected political turmoil. Although China will not have any major disputes at present, it is still dangerous not to find ways to coordinate labor and capital and seek appropriate solutions.

(5) Revitalize agriculture and do not focus on industry. In the past, because China was based on agriculture, I advocated supporting the development of industry and commerce. Now, with new knowledge gained from the facts, I believe that without revitalizing agriculture, there is no way to support industry. Because without agriculture, industry has no raw materials, and farmers have no purchasing power. Therefore, revitalizing agriculture is an important vital element in supporting industry. Moreover, the majority of the Chinese population is farmers. If we want China to be peaceful, we must revitalize agriculture.

Interview Record

A Conversation with Mr. Wu Yun Chu, Who Recently Returned from Europe and America

— Qiacheng

"Why has 'Ajinomoto' disappeared from the market?"

This, of course, must be attributed to the invention of monosodium glutamate (MSG). The invention of domestic substitutes is much more effective than slogans and declarations boycotting foreign goods! Therefore, in this freezing weather, I still visited Mr. Wu Yun Chu, the inventor of MSG, with enthusiasm.

After being led to the office, I met Mr. Wu, who had gray hair and a dusty face, and it was obvious that he had returned from Europe and America. There was no decoration in the room, and newly boxed goods were piled up outside. There were several guest lists and some planning books on the desk. There were also several male and female employees working in the room, but only the sound of machines from the neighboring room broke the silence here. What people care about most is naturally MSG, so the first sentence I asked directly was:

"Mr. Wu, can you talk to me about MSG?"

"Okay! But that's just a transitional business." It was also an unadorned answer.

"When did you start doing it?"

After some material examination, I found in a small booklet: "It was in 1922!" It was still a simple answer.

"What was the process like?"

"At first, I used chemical methods to analyze its ingredients from Japanese condiments, and then I used these ingredients to re-match and try it. At the beginning, the cost was very high and it was not suitable for commercial transactions. After three months, it was successful after several improvements."

"Does Mr. Wu operate other businesses besides Tianchu MSG now?"

"There are also Tianyuan Electrochemical Plant and Chi Chang New Company, which specializes in the raw materials for making matches."

Facing such an interviewee, I was really a little overwhelmed, but after my shifting exploration, his talkativeness could be elicited.

"Mr. Wu, what are your impressions after investigating in Europe and America?"

"I think our chemical industry should do basic work, but the interest is a little weaker. It seems not very cost-effective in terms of business. Fortunately, Tianchu has been strong recently, so I took on this responsibility myself. Regarding the work of manufacturing green gas, it has already started, and after the layout is in place, it can be started. At the same time, the work of light gas is also underway. I have also discussed with many experts abroad, and the plan has been successful. Because the war in the near future is a material war, the industrial sector must take into account national defense and make industrial military."

After saying that, he added a few more sentences: "This kind of business is based on obligation, not for the sake of rights. However, businessmen aim to make profits, so I have already made detailed budgets for this event before it started."

When talking about the impressions of the investigation, he told a lot about the situation of the international industrial sector recently. He still used simple and unadorned words from the low and slow sound belt to express it. When talking about China's future, Mr. Wu's opinion was:

"When I was abroad, I debated with many foreigners who despised China. I said, if China can work hard for ten years and everyone cooperate and divide the work, there is always great hope; but if we fight each other like this, it is hard to say."

When I was saying goodbye, he unexpectedly said to me:

"Please don't talk too much about MSG, because this is not considered an achievement, and I don't want to have excessive publicity." Because Mr. Wu has more valuable contributions (making acid and alkali). In the rattling of the machines, I walked out of the factory and threw myself back into the noisy downtown.

National Goods Forum

Exhibition and Sale

— Pan Yang An

A guest returned from visiting the exhibition of products from the Shanghai Products Association at the Zhizhi Expo and praised, "The preciousness of the products, the richness of the collection, and the beauty of the display are incomparable to the previous disorganization or deliberate shelving and non-display. However, speaking of the shortcomings, there are many treasures inside that are not for sale, and there is regret that people cannot buy them even if they want to. As for the China National Products Company, it gathers the essence of various factories, and strives to collect them without any effort, but there are still many daily necessities that have not been able to do everything that should be done." His words were very sincere. I responded by saying, "Your words are good, but you don't fully understand the purpose of it. Please let me finish what I have to say: The purpose of the exhibition is to promote people's attention, arouse people's feelings, and encourage manufacturers to improve their technology and induce buyers to love domestic products. Therefore, the display of its products should be fine rather than broad, and emphasize display rather than sales. Sometimes, using scientific methods, the order of products is listed for the reference of viewers. Sometimes, rare treasures are exhibited from a historical perspective to broaden the observation of viewers. Sometimes, with the means of foreign trade, we cater to the customs of foreigners to expand overseas sales. Sometimes, with international friendship, we specially make characters worshiped and loved by foreigners to make gifts of friendship. This is the true purpose of the exhibition. It is not originally a business principle, nor is it just to attract customers and attract customers. It contains an advertising effect only. Therefore, there are non-selling products and selling products in the exhibition venue, which can be freely chosen by the exhibitors without restrictions. However, in non-selling products, in addition to unparalleled antiques and rare treasures, categories can also be designated and specially customized. Even among the selling products, according to the exhibition method, they must be taken out after the end of the exhibition period. There are very few who sell them arbitrarily to disrupt the order of the venue. As for the China National Products Company, since it is not an exhibition in nature, everything displayed in the company is a selling product, and there is nothing that cannot be taken and delivered to the customer at any time. The display of its products emphasizes both fine and broad, beautiful and cheap. At the beginning of its operation, there was indeed the regret that the collection was not universal and the supply was not abundant. Recently, those in charge of it have realized this and have embraced the idea of opening up more doors. All fine and pure domestic products are included in the sales. Recently, it has also announced in the newspaper to solicit goods, aiming to gather famous products from various places and complete the needs of daily use, hoping that from a needle and a thread to a piece of paper, to fox fur, mink fur, mountain treasures, and seafood, customers can enter the door of the National Products Company, and everything they need to eat, what they lack to wear, and even daily necessities in their homes and necessities for travel are available to satisfy the wishes of customers and satiate the hearts of those who love to use domestic products. This is the ambition of the National Products Company. Bearing this mission and following the established goal, I hope that in the near future, every customer will be satisfied and happy, and have the joy of being at home. The guest heard my words, nodded and left, and used the above narration to inform the readers, and I would like to encourage the exhibition hall and the colleagues of the National Products Company."

National Goods News

Suzhou's Promotion of National Products is Hot

— Jia Hua

Since the Shanghai National Products community designated this year as the National Products Year and established the China National Products Company, Sanwu has taken the lead in the trend. Through the vigorous promotion of industrial and commercial leaders and local gentry, the National Products Movement in Suzhou has suddenly shown a lively image. Therefore, the information I heard is summarized as follows.

(Sudden Rise of National Products Market) The gentry and merchants of Suzhou had a plan to establish a National Products Market. After half a year of preparation, it coincided with the Japanese invasion of Shanghai. The situation was chaotic and people were panicking, so the progress was stopped. At the beginning of this year, under the urging of the National Products Promotion Committee of the Wuxian Chamber of Commerce, a meeting was convened again and the original site of the North Bureau Fire Brigade was surveyed and determined to be rebuilt into a market. As for the fire brigade, another nearby Lvqiufang Alley was found. All the relocation conditions were generally agreed upon. The authorized capital of the market is 120,000 yuan, which is entirely used for building houses. Two-thirds of it has been recognized by the initiators and various trade associations. The remaining one-third will be publicly solicited. Recently, due to the cost of preparation, the initiators have pre-funded 20,000 yuan to carry out the project quite actively. It is expected that construction will start after February. Roughly, a complete National Products Market can be established in the new city center of the North Bureau during the Lunar New Year to meet the needs of the people of Suzhou.

(Enthusiastic Broadcasting and Speeches) The Wuxian County Chamber of Commerce has an organization of the National Products Promotion Committee. Those in charge of it are all industrial and commercial leaders of Sanwu. In the past, the work was quite restricted due to funding. This year, after Shanghai designated it as the National Products Year, the work suddenly became tense. Starting from the 18th of last month, a National Products broadcasting lecture was held at the Wu's Sarala Flower Hall Radio Station for 63 days. The speakers were all well-known people in Sanwu and National Products industrial and commercial leaders. The 5th of this month was the 16th day. Zhang Yipeng, a famous figure in the French Concession, gave a lecture. When talking about the situation of foreign goods dumping and economic aggression, he almost burst into tears. He also sang a song on the broadcasting station. The lyrics said. Speaking of promoting National Products.. It's hard for me to feel good.. The clothes are wool and cotton cloth.. The food is tobacco, alcohol, and candy.. The houses have windows.. The cars and railways run.. The four elements of life.. All rely on other people's help.. Plus guns, cannons, and military fire.. Spend money like dirt.. Flip through the customs account books.. Countless money flows out.. Everyone quickly wakes up.. Must rely on your own ability.. Quickly discard foreign goods.. Quickly protect rights.. Strictly block dumping policies.. Break economic aggression.. Don't be a five-minute fever.. Don't make a big mistake.. I am now talking with good intentions.. Save the tragedy of national subjugation..

(Preparation for Fashion Exhibition) Zhang Shoupeng, chairman of the National Products Promotion Committee, recently told reporters that the association's future work policy is: First, to awaken women with higher consumption, and second, to instill in innocent and lively children. This is the first step in promoting National Products. It is now planned to hold a grand fashion exhibition to awaken the attention of men and women to the characteristics of National Products, and to hold a county-wide speech contest for school-age children, so as to instill the true meaning and significance of promoting National Products into the minds of school-age children, so that they will not be confused by glamorous foreign goods when they grow up. However, the above two tasks are planned to be held during the summer vacation due to economic and time reasons, so that the clothing for the fashion exhibition can save some expenses, and the speech contest can be held without wasting studies. Although there is this proposal now, it has not yet been carried out. But no matter what, a meeting will be convened this month to put it forward for discussion and actively prepare for it.

A National Match Company Worth Introducing

— Hong Ni

As the saying goes, a single spark can start a prairie fire. Although matches are a small daily necessity, they are indirectly related to people's livelihoods. Don't look down on matches as a small matter of two or three copper coins a pack. Accumulating them, the number is quite considerable. Just in terms of match unified tax, the total national annual amount has reached millions of taels, and the import volume of foreign matches, according to customs statistics, is at least more than 20 million taels. The factories established in China to avoid import taxes are not included. Before the January 28th Incident, we could see Phoenix brand matches being sold everywhere in China, especially Shanghai, which was the general hub for the sales of Phoenix brand matches. Domestic matches were in danger of closing down due to the dumping of foreign goods and the squeezing of donations and taxes. Soon after the suicide of Krueger, known as the Match King, the Phoenix brand matches also gradually decreased in power in China due to this reason. The Great China Match Company of domestic matches, which came out of the Beautiful brand (that is, the famous cigarette brand), seized the opportunity to succeed the Phoenix brand and sell well in the country.

The Great China Match Company was founded in the autumn of 1930. It was a merger of Yingchang, Hongsheng, Zhonghua, and Yusheng Companies. General Manager Liu Hongsheng hired Dr. Lin Tianji of chemistry, selected domestic raw materials, and used the latest scientific methods to make medicated stem matches, such as the Beautiful, Golden Rooster, Insurance, and Five Bats brands of matches, which are no less than foreign matches. Manufacturing factories were set up in Shanghai, Hankou, Ganzhen, and Suzhou, using self-made stem pieces. The annual turnover reached several million. The capital has recently increased to more than three million. In our country, it can be regarded as the first. By analogy, we can know that even the smallest things cannot be spared by luck. I specially record it to introduce it to the readers.

National Goods Talk

What Makes a Sound National Products Salesperson

— Jin Song Tang

For the operation of all industries and businesses, in addition to the soundness of the internal organization and the excellence of the products, the handling of business affairs and the improvement of external sales are certainly also a major key. Salespeople bear the mission of entrusting the entire business of a company and have a close relationship with a company. It is conceivable that they should work hard to promote it. Now that imported goods are rampant and domestic products are declining, what should salespeople in the National Products business pay more attention to? Based on what I have seen, I would like to discuss it with you.

In the old days, in our country's old shops, those who were in charge of business affairs (commonly known as "street runners") were often the manager or shop assistant of a shop. Most of these people had no firm goals and no sufficient experience. As for the discerning eyes and the agile skills, let alone. So, day after day, year after year, they were content with the status quo and stagnated. There were many who went bankrupt due to slow turnover and those who stopped business due to bad debts. As for witnessing the influx of foreign goods, they only shouted and complained, but did not seek to resist the enemy. In recent years, industry and commerce have flourished and the level of social knowledge has increased. The general old-fashioned street runners have been eliminated. However, it is as rare as phoenix feathers to find a salesperson with a pure new idea and principle. I have served in the industrial and commercial sector for more than ten years. After examining the actual experience, I have accumulated the following points. I feel that National Products salespeople should have these indispensable conditions. I will list them one by one below. A. Dignified Attitude and Conduct Salespeople represent a company when dealing with outsiders. A stable attitude and clear speech will prevent the other party from having bad images and lead to contempt. Salespeople are responsible for activities, not as mechanical as the work of internal personnel. Therefore, there is more contact with society, and the adverse external environment and bad customs often cause salespeople to degenerate too much. They should have a clear mind and strong credibility, so as not to go with the flow and be despised by others. If one is unfavorable to oneself, the company will also suffer damage to its reputation.

B. Firm and Rich Will and Knowledge Since attitude and conduct need to be dignified, will and knowledge should also be sufficient. Salespeople should make decisive decisions and have a clear hierarchy in the process of external business contacts, cargo loading, and payment collection. Avoid perfunctory treatment and frequent misunderstandings. Other things, such as business habits and economic conditions, should be well-informed. If the will is firm, the foothold is stable, and if the knowledge is rich, you will not fall behind.

C. Flexible Eyes and Skills Attitude, conduct, will, and knowledge can already be dealt with, but without deep and sharp eyes and agile skills, it is also in vain. The people encountered by salespeople are from all over the country. They go in different directions, and their dialects are different, and their habits are different. Without clever activities and adapting to circumstances, how can we seek to promote products and generate transactions?

D. Value of Conversation and Observation In this time of rural collapse and financial depression, the position of industry and commerce is in a precarious state. In addition, inland merchants have insufficient intelligence and scattered organizations. The customer accounts of the industrial and commercial sector are like candles in the wind. Therefore, salespeople's conversations with customers have the value of careful attention. Whether the store is well-established and what the internal situation is, do not hesitate to speak and write it down for reference to the release of accounts. It is also a shortcut to credit investigation, and business operations will benefit greatly from this.

E. The Spirit of Endurance and Hard Work There is a need for scrutiny between the salesperson's responses and in the socializing, but the spirit of enduring and enduring hardship is also an essential element for salespeople. Even in the scorching sun, sweating like rain, and in the cold winter, with the wind blowing in the face, we should go every day and work hard, so as to avoid the separation of information and the weakening of feelings.

In this autumn of commercial warfare competition, success or failure depends entirely on planning and proper handling. Salespeople who can endure hardship, not mind the trouble of talking, and not be afraid of the cold, heat, wind, and rain, should be courteous in their responses, fluent and lively in their speech, solemn and sincere in their attitude, and clear and firm in their thinking, not corrupt, and not perfunctory. That is an element of success, and the future of National Products is deeply reliant on it.

A Word to the Three Major Companies

— Wan Gong

Shanghai is the central hub for imported goods. The department stores that gather the greatest variety of imports must surely be Sincere, Wing On, and Sun Sun, right? Their store signs and advertisements all prominently display the phrase "Dealing in Global Merchandise." Isn't this irrefutable proof that they promote imported goods? Seeing these signs, I couldn't help but gasp!

Promoting national goods is, of course, the responsibility of all citizens. But if merchants don't sell them, where are people supposed to buy them? True, they'll argue, "Because there are buyers, there will be sellers." However, the young masters and modern ladies who insist on foreign goods are ultimately a minority. Ordinary people don't inherently favor foreign goods over domestic ones. It's just that the marketplace is filled with foreign products, so they casually buy them. There are many people like this. There are also those who are enthusiastic about promoting national goods and want to use them but struggle to find them and lack the ability to distinguish between them. Isn't this the merchants' responsibility?

Therefore, when it comes to promoting national goods, merchants should be on the front lines, especially the famous major companies in Shanghai. While they can't be expected to stop selling foreign goods altogether, they should also consider the phrase "Promote Chinese Local Products" on their store signs. Their display windows should primarily showcase national goods, and unless customers specifically request foreign products, they should present domestic goods first. If these major companies all actively promoted national goods, I believe the impact would be significant. Finally, I hope that the three major companies will be inspired by their conscience and, like the China National Goods Company, implement national goods to save the country. I would gladly walk past your doors every day and offer a salute!

Spring and Autumn

Butterfly Talk

— Zhan Lu

The longest-lived butterfly in the world is undoubtedly the Immortal Butterfly in the Imperial Ancestral Temple of old Beijing. Yellow in color and as large as a teacup, it is said to have lived since the Jiajing reign of the Ming dynasty, making it a long-lived butterfly of three or four hundred years. Emperor Qianlong of the Qing dynasty even wrote a poem about the Immortal Butterfly of the Imperial Ancestral Temple. Later, the Immortal Butterfly would occasionally appear, and books such as "Records of the Capital City" and "Hong Xue Yin Yuan" all document it.

The best-flying butterflies in the world come from two locations: one is the large white butterfly produced on the islands of the Baltic Sea, called "Cabbage White," which often forms long-distance traveling groups, flying to various European countries. When they pass by, they resemble scattered and enlarged snowflakes in the air. The other is the pink butterfly produced in central Africa, known as "Snow Maiden," whose flying ability is even more astonishing! They can fly across the Sahara Desert in the thousands and hundreds, and after circling in North Africa for several days, they still have the strength to continue flying north to the prosperous British Isles.

Recently, I read "Planting Hermitage Collection" by Li Zixin of Dantu, which records the chaos of the Taiping Rebellion. Jiangdu He Guiqing held troops in Changzhou, planning to recover lost territory. Suddenly, a large colorful butterfly flew to the governor's office. He thought it was an immortal envoy descending to earth, so he immediately set up an incense table, dressed in formal attire, and bowed to the butterfly, asking about the safety of the situation. Those who flattered He all said this was a sign of a triumphant return. Later, the main camp collapsed, and He abandoned his post and fled. At that time, the national law was still strict, and generals who lost battles could not escape punishment. Li Zixin has a "Butterfly Song" published in his collection, which includes the warning sentence: "The battle gates are wide open, flags unfurl, the envoy's crown and belt shine in the office, the three armies cheer, moving heaven and earth, the flower and bird envoy comes to Penglai... The envoy is always mindful of the military and the country, burning incense to ask the butterfly about gains and losses, only wishing to seek fragrance and be drunk, protecting the good spring scenery of Jiangnan..."

Chronic and Acute

— Xian Xian

丨Chronic is Still Better丨

In the past, two doctors with queues and tight sleeves argued, nearly cracking each other's heads open. One was a Confucian doctor from a seven-generation family, what society calls a Chinese doctor. The other was a recent graduate of a medical university in Europe. Although he was also a genuine, old-fashioned, and unadulterated Chinese, society called him a foreign doctor. The reason for their conflict was that the Chinese doctor said the foreign doctor didn't understand pulse diagnosis, and the foreign doctor said the Chinese doctor didn't know anatomy. You call me an abscess, I call you a bastard. Later, a busybody peacemaker came out to mediate, saying that Chinese medicine is relatively stable, and Western medicine is relatively quick. It's like crossing a mountain: Chinese medicine likes to walk on the constructed road, and Western medicine likes to take the shortcut through the thorny bushes. Each has its own strengths, and each takes its own path. Fortunately, they reach the same destination by different routes, so there's no need for the rich to be intolerant of the poor.

The above story seems like a joke, but it fully demonstrates the chronic nature of China and the acute nature of foreign countries. Recently, I have obtained many more examples of chronic and acute. Taking walking as an example, Chinese people always like to swagger on the cement, while foreigners are always in a hurry, as if their butts are on fire. In the past, we often saw Chinese people walking in front of foreigners being pushed aside by foreigners and rushing past. Now, this rude and insulting behavior is not often seen, perhaps because the level of Chinese people has increased or because foreigners have become more civilized. However, foreigners behind Chinese people still often overtake them. Similarly, when facing national crises, people always run and jump, while Chinese people prefer to move slowly to ensure stability and plan for all contingencies.

Someone said that foreigners are impatient and Chinese people are slow. According to you, China's demise will also be relatively slow. Is that correct? I said, perhaps there is some truth to it.

Spring Has Arrived

— Ye Zi

丨Springtime Guangxi Youth丨

What I want to talk about here is the scene of young men and women in Ping Le, He County, Zhong Shan, Zhao Ping and other counties in Guangxi province during springtime. Although I dare not say that they can represent the entire province, I always feel that they can at least represent the majority.

Once spring arrives, they have a lot of free time. Whether rich or poor, they spend their time leisurely in the first and second months of the year. Therefore, on market days, there are always traces of their red and green figures. Sometimes they run to the foot of the mountain or the riverbank to sing "mountain songs." Men and women respond to each other, and it is said that some of those songs are extremely sad, even making them and their partners cry. But some are also extremely joyous. Imagine Guangxi, where the climate is mild. Once spring arrives, everywhere is a scene of faces and peach blossoms reflecting each other in rosy hues. Naturally, these young men and women also take advantage of their youth to burn the flames of love! Most of the songs are love songs. Unfortunately, I cannot remember those good songs, so I can only copy down the two that I can currently remember, which are not very good:

"Love, ah! (Note) Sit, just sit,

Sit on the hilltop and sing a song.

Brother sings a line, sister sings a line,

Everyone sings until the osmanthus blossoms."

(Note) Meaning "love."

"If you love a sister, love a tender girl,

If you love a brother, love a young man;

Older brother is like a money tree,

Younger sister is like an embroidered bed."

If the men and women sing very well together, then they will enjoy each other in mountain caves or secluded places, or the woman will follow the man to a thatched hut or empty house in the wilderness to enjoy each other, staying for several days perhaps. However, some are not out of the woman's willingness, often forced by the man. It is said that women always "pretend to lower their heads when they have intentions in their hearts."
